Special Report

A Simple Explanation of Shanghai's Anti-Smoking Propaganda 143

A. The Origin of the Opium Evil

Opium is produced in India and was first imported into our country during the early Qing Dynasty. At that time, the people of the whole country were unaware of the harm of opium and regarded it as a recreational product. Who knew that under these circumstances, unknowingly, it would lure many of our compatriots into the sea of suffering, creating irresolvable pain. From then on, the import of opium increased day by day, and its poisonous effects spread throughout the country. At this time, the Qing court also knew that the harm of opium was too great and could not bear to see it spread. Therefore, in the eighteenth year of Daoguang, Lin Zexu was ordered to go to Guangdong to handle the prohibition of opium, arrest opium merchants, and confiscate property. Because the measures were too radical, it triggered the Opium War and the signing of many unequal treaties, which placed our country under heavy constraints, and we have not been able to relax until now. After this setback, not only did the import of opium become greater than before, but the national power also weakened day by day. Looking back now, we truly feel a pain so deep that we have no tears to shed.

B. The Harms of Opium

From a broad perspective, there are approximately the following types:

(1) Affecting the country's economy. In recent years, China's economy has entered a state of bankruptcy, which is an undeniable fact. Although there are more than one reason for this, the import of opium and other narcotics, this shocking drain, must also be considered a major fatal blow. According to a customs investigation in 1926, more than 40 million taels were imported from India, and more than 18 million boxes of red soil were imported from Persia. In addition, the import of morphine, cocaine, heroin, and other drugs also amounted to more than 1 million taels. Furthermore, according to a survey in Dalian alone, 698,897 taels of opium were imported into that place, with a value of over a million. The total amount of outflow is more than ten million yuan. China was originally a country with a trade deficit. Adding this huge amount of outflow, how can the national economy not go bankrupt? How can people's livelihoods not be difficult? If we want to restore our rights and interests and cultivate a bit of vitality for the country, we only have one way: to ban opium!

(2) Affecting the country's health. In any nation, if there are too many smokers, that nation will inevitably weaken. This is an irrefutable law. Because mentally weak smokers will inevitably not produce physically healthy children. If this is passed down from generation to generation, the spirit of the entire nation will inevitably be invisibly eliminated. The reason why our Chinese nation is not valued by foreigners and is called the "sick man of East Asia" is because there are too many smokers and their spirits are not invigorated. If we want to maintain our nation and always occupy a place in the era of survival of the fittest, we must first ban opium, which is harmful to health!

(3) Affecting the nation's status. Since the import of opium into our country, many anti-smoking regulations have been signed with foreign countries over the years, such as the "Regulations on the Prohibition of the Transport of Morphine, Opium, and Drug Needles" in the thirty-fourth year of Guangxu in the former Qing Dynasty, the "Chapter on the Prohibition and Restriction of Morphine into China" in the third year of Xuantong, the International Opium Convention of the Hague Peace Conference in the second year of the Republic of China, and the successive meetings of the Narcotics Committee of the League of Nations, etc. However, the domestic opium ban is still lax, and poppies are everywhere, which has brought international credibility and the nation's status to an unimaginable level. It is also remembered that in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China, our country's representatives passed the proposal of the British Far East Opium Investigation Group at the Geneva International Anti-Smoking Conference. This is all great evidence. If our people still do not realize this and still regard this harmful opium as a pastime, the future disasters will not only be the decline of the nation's status!

(4) Affecting social order. As the saying goes, "When a person is poor, his ambitions are short." This means that when a person is at the end of his rope and has no money to use, he will do anything, even join a gang of thieves. We cannot attribute the cause of poverty entirely to opium use. Many crimes in cities have nothing to do with smoking. However, a person who uses opium will sooner or later embark on a path of poverty. Therefore, all illegal and immoral things are decided when puffing smoke in the opium den. Therefore, the maintenance of social order depends on how many poor people there are in this society. In other words, if there are more opium smokers in this society, even if it is not visible for a while, it will affect the future. People who smoke like this will inevitably reach the end of their road and be unable to be saved. Therefore, from the standpoint of social order, we must abandon this important factor that causes social poverty and crime.

(5) Affecting the people's food supply. Anyone who has been to Sichuan and Yunnan knows that the farmland in these provinces has mostly been converted to growing opium poppies in recent years, and agricultural crops are regarded as by-products. Therefore, the output of opium has increased day by day, and the output of rice and wheat will naturally decrease day by day. How can the domestic food supply not be lacking? China is known as an agricultural country, and an agricultural country cannot even maintain its own food supply and must rely on foreign countries. Needless to say, this is entirely due to the influence of opium cultivation.

From a small perspective, there are approximately the following types:

(1) Harming one's personal health. People who smoke opium are always lying in bed all day long, living a life of indulgence and ignoring day and night. All their energy and brainpower are absorbed by the opium poison. On the physical side, it is of course impossible to talk about being strong and lively, and they will also show an indescribably haggard appearance. Therefore, it is not too harsh to ridicule smokers as "opium ghosts." People who are addicted to opium are simply digging their own graves and seeking their own death.

(2) Losing one's personal wealth. People who smoke opium may only be indulging in a pastime at first and do not think about the economic losses. However, after becoming addicted, they feel that they cannot stop. Knowing that it costs money, they have to endure the pain with peace of mind. Unconsciously, they squander all their family property. In the end, some become beggars, and some become thieves. There are countless such common occurrences. How heartbreaking this is!

(3) Destroying family happiness. The reason why a family is harmonious and prosperous is that each person can take responsibility to work and earn money. If one person does not engage in honest work and becomes addicted to opium, not only will there be one more useless person in the family, but production will inevitably decrease, and expenses will increase even more. Over time, the economy will inevitably go bankrupt, and even family members may become strangers, and husbands and wives may become resentful. Even unexpected tragedies may occur. Because one person smokes opium, the happiness of the entire family is affected. The harm of opium is so severe, why not make a decision to get rid of it?

C. Determination and Steps for Banning Opium

The poisonous effects of opium are enough to destroy our country and wipe out our nation. Since Lin Zexu's implementation of the opium ban failed, whether it was the Qing court or the Northern Warlords, they have continued to promote the opium ban. But why has the opium ban not been eradicated until now? There are only two reasons: (1) The government does not have the determination to completely ban opium. (2) The government does not have practical and feasible methods for banning opium. Because the past opium bans only had clauses on punishing opium users, but did not have fundamental measures to eradicate opium seedlings and prohibit planting and smoking in stages. Therefore, the production of opium has increased year by year, and the number of smokers has also increased year by year. Now, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has indeed made the greatest determination on the item of opium prohibition, starting from the root and adopting the six-year opium eradication plan decided by the previous National Congress. It has been decided that the period from this year to 1940 shall be the eradication period. In addition to strictly stipulating regulations and prohibiting planting in stages, the two most effective methods are adopted to prohibit opium use. One is to promote the New Life Movement to change social customs and encourage the people to assist the government in banning opium. The other is to use scientific methods under the extremely fair and extremely systematic principles to make smokers quit smoking in stages. The first step is to hold a general registration of smokers nationwide, to know the total number of smokers nationwide, as a standard for reducing the number of smokers year by year. This city has adhered to the government's opium prohibition plan and has already registered in July. From July to the end of September is the period for voluntary registration. During this period, people are allowed to voluntarily surrender for rehabilitation or obtain a license. From October to the end of December is the period for mandatory registration. During this period, the arrest of private smokers will begin, and fines will be imposed according to law. After that, mandatory registration will be carried out. Regarding the opium prohibition steps, they are set to be six years in accordance with the government's plan, from this year to 1940. The steps are: (1) From July to November 1935, register smokers and issue limited-term smoking cessation licenses. (2) From 1936, the issuance of limited-term smoking cessation licenses will be stopped. At least one-fifth of all registered smokers must quit. Those who have not quit will exchange for new licenses. (3) In 1937, at least two-fifths of the registered and licensed smokers must quit. Those who have not quit will exchange for new licenses. (4) In 1938, at least three-fifths of the registered and licensed smokers must quit. Those who have not quit will exchange for new licenses. (5) In 1939, at least four-fifths of the registered and licensed smokers must quit. Those who have not quit will exchange for new licenses. (6) In 1940, all registered and licensed smokers must quit, and the smoking cessation licenses will be handed in for cancellation.

D. The Meaning and Procedures of Registration

(1) Why register? The call for banning opium has been going on for decades. Although it is not heard everywhere and at all times, the result is still that those who ban it ban it, and those who smoke it smoke it. This is of course inevitable as a means of collecting money in the era of warlords, and it is also because there are no perfect methods. Now the government has seen that the past opium bans have not achieved considerable results, so in considering both sides, it has come up with a registration method. Because to implement the opium ban, the first step is to know the total number of smokers in the country. In the total number, we must further analyze how many young people there are, how many middle-aged people there are, and how many elderly people there are. Only by obtaining this statistics can we gradually advance and reduce the number of smokers year by year, so that ordinary smokers can quit comfortably without any pain. If we still use the past method of no statistics and do not give smokers a considerable amount of time to quit, we want to immediately eradicate opium, which has been poisonous for decades, which is absolutely impossible in reality. Therefore, the government asserts that the most effective method of banning opium and the most painless way for smokers to quit is registration.

(2) What are the benefits of registration? The so-called registration is not about getting a license and becoming an official opium smoker, and no one will interfere with you anymore. If you have this kind of thinking, then this is a big mistake. You must know that smoker registration, on the one hand, is the government expressing its determination to ban opium and awakening the attention of smokers, and on the other hand, it is to make registered smokers know how many years are left for the smoking period, and to gradually reduce the amount of smoking according to their own smoking amount, so that they can quit as scheduled, get out of the sea of ​​suffering, and become a healthy citizen. Or if you feel the pain of smoking, you can immediately ask the Public Security Bureau to send you to the Municipal Smoking Cessation Hospital, which will help you quit for free. Only registered smokers can get this kind of preferential treatment.

(3) What are the disadvantages of not registering? This time, the government's implementation of the opium ban has a very great determination, not like the past, when it was just a matter of following the story to cover up one's eyes and ears. The reason why we want to register first is to take into account the actual difficulties and eliminate the pain of smokers. If smokers do not understand the government's determination and kindness, and still wait and see, treating it as a ban on opium that has been followed many times in the past, in the future, after the registration time has passed, not only will they not be able to apply for registration again, but they will also not be able to get free smoking cessation, and if they are found out, they will be severely punished. Smokers, think about it carefully, what is the point of this? Do you really want to be forever mired in the sea of ​​suffering, willing to be a despicable person who is not tolerated by the country and despised by compatriots?

(4) Registration Procedures

All registration matters are handled by the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Anyone applying for an ordinary smoking cessation license must first fill out a registration application form and go to the Public Security Bureau or its sub-bureaus to apply for registration. The Public Security Bureau or its sub-bureaus will issue a license based on the filled form. As for those who apply for a poor people's license, in addition to filling out an application form, they must also provide a guarantee letter. After an investigator is sent to investigate, a poor people's license will be issued. As for those who request smoking cessation, they must also fill out an application form and guarantee letter. After the investigation is clear, they will be sent to a smoking cessation hospital for free treatment.

The Municipal Public Security Bureau, in consideration of the difficulty for smokers to find a guarantor, has specially stipulated the qualifications of the guarantor. All relatives and friends of the smoker who have a confirmed address and a proper profession can serve as guarantors. It is not necessary to find a shop guarantor. The guarantor of the poor people's smoking cessation license only needs to guarantee that the smoker is not impersonating a poor person. The guarantor of those who request smoking cessation only needs to guarantee that the smoker will not deliberately evade when they are summoned for investigation after being discharged from the hospital, and there is no other responsibility. Therefore, there is no need to worry too much about serving as a guarantor for a smoker.

E. Hope for Opium Prohibition

(1) Hope for smokers. People who smoke opium should know that the harm of opium is not only a great loss to personal reputation and career, but also a great impact on the country and the nation. It is hoped that smokers will regard quitting opium as the most pleasant and beneficial thing, because after the opium addiction is removed, they can restore their health and become a useful citizen. On the personal side, they will no longer be looked down upon. On the national side, they can also be revived from now on.

(2) Hope for planters and sellers. People who plant and sell opium should know that this kind of business is not legitimate and is illegal. Once found out, the punishment is even more severe than that of unregistered smokers. Why do you do this kind of thing that is harmful to others and not beneficial to yourself? It is hoped that you will change the land used for planting opium to planting grains as soon as possible, and that you will find other businesses for the capital used to sell opium. Do not try it lightly again and become a victim under this opium prohibition order.

(3) Hope for the general public. It is of course very good for people who do not smoke opium, but it is not considered to be fulfilling the responsibilities of a citizen to the fullest if they hold a principle of taking care of themselves alone and see others smoking as if it has nothing to do with them. Because whether it is a country or a society, it is made up of a majority of people. If there are too many smokers, this country and society cannot be healthy. Even if they are not directly harmed by opium, they will also be greatly affected indirectly. It is hoped that everyone will earnestly persuade relatives, friends, or related people who smoke opium. It is best to quit immediately, otherwise, persuade them to register quickly. By pooling our efforts, we can assist the government in gradually completing the important task of opium prohibition. This is the way to be a citizen.

Our final slogans are: 1. Opium prohibition is the best way to stop social leakage and save the poor. 2. Opium prohibition is a prerequisite for the revival of the nation. 3. Opium prohibition is an important strategy to restore international status. 4. Opium prohibition is the original plan to strengthen the country and the race. 5. Opium prohibition is the most determined and hard-working important task of the government at present. 6. Opium prohibition is the basic plan for implementing the New Life Movement. 7. It is hoped that compatriots across the country will unanimously assist the work of opium prohibition. Issued by the Shanghai Anti-Smoking Committee and the Shanghai Public Security Bureau.

Anti-Smoking Slogans

(1) The harm of opium is greater than floods and ferocious beasts. (2) Opium is a poisonous substance that destroys life, bankrupts families, destroys countries, and exterminates races. (3) Smoking opium is a violation of the law at all times. (4) People with opium addiction will never be loyal and hardworking. (5) People with opium addiction will never abide by the time when doing things. (6) Shop assistants with opium addiction will never have integrity. (7) Quitting opium addiction is like walking from a dead end to a life path. (8) Quitting opium addiction is to get rid of the burden of your life. (9) If opium addiction is not quit, no one will use you in the future. (10) If opium is banned, the country's poverty and weakness will have a turning point. (11) If opium is banned, the international status can be increased. (12) Banning opium is Premier Sun Yat-sen's most important legacy of saving the country. (13) Banning opium is the policy of the government's greatest determination. (14) Smokers, come and register quickly to avoid arrest and punishment. (15) Smokers, ask for smoking cessation, no money, no pain. (16) Smoker registration is the first step in the opium prohibition work. (17) Smoker registration is to seek the total number of smokers, as a standard for gradual reduction year by year. (18) Registration is the right of smokers and the most stable method. The registration certificate is the necessary guarantee for smokers at present.

Anti-Smoking Public Notice (for films)

Now the government is determined to ban opium and has set a deadline of six years to eradicate it. People who smoke opium and cannot quit temporarily should quickly go to the Municipal Public Security Bureau and its sub-bureaus to register and obtain a license. If you are determined to quit opium, you can apply to be sent to the smoking cessation hospital for treatment immediately, which will not cost you a penny. Smoking is illegal, but registering and obtaining a license can avoid penalties. Waiting and hesitating is to trap yourself in the net of law. Propaganda Group of the Shanghai Anti-Smoking Committee, Shanghai Public Security Bureau, issued.

A Private Morphine Manufacturing Facility Was Cracked Down in Dafu Lane, Maizhi Road. Five People, Including the Shareholding Boss, Were Arrested, and More Than One Hundred Taels of Wet and Dry Materials Were Confiscated. 144

Zhang Ziying, a detective from the special agency of the French Concession Police Department, learned yesterday morning that someone had privately set up a morphine manufacturing facility in the house at No. 7, Dafu Lane, No. 24 Maizhi Road, secretly manufacturing and selling it to various places, making a lot of profit. The detective reported to Inspector Jin Jiulin, and at 1:30 PM, he, together with Western detectives, led a team of detectives, including Bu Zhenglong, Xu Jinlong, Zhu Jutong, Tao Ronglin, and Zuo Qihong, rushed to the address. Seeing that the house at that number was a two-story building, they first guarded the front and back doors, and then knocked on the door and entered. The entire second floor and the pavilion were used as workplaces, equipped with several electric motors of various sizes. The workers were working hard, which was indeed a large-scale manufacturing facility. The shareholding bosses Cai Henian (from Shanghai), Cai Asheng (from Pudong), Liu Ziming (from Ningbo), the buddies Zhou Xinlai (from Ningbo), Gu Axia, and other five people were arrested on the spot, and more than one hundred taels of morphine and raw materials used for manufacturing were confiscated. It was estimated that the value of the equipment, assets, and goods of the facility was approximately more than ten thousand gold. The suspects and stolen goods were taken back to the police station for interrogation, and will be sent to the Second Special Court for trial today. Detectives were sent to guard the facility, to arrest accomplices, and craftsmen were hired to dismantle the motor parts and transport them to the police station for verification.

In the Shanghai-Hong Kong interport tennis Taggart Cup, Shanghai won two more groups against Hong Kong yesterday, one singles and one doubles, totaling four wins for Shanghai, continuing to hold the Taggart Cup. Today's second singles match between Li Huitang and D'Orfeu is irrelevant to the championship. The Shanghai-Hong Kong interport competition has been won by Shanghai since 1931. Except for last year when there was no competition, it has won four consecutive editions. In yesterday's first women's singles match, Hong Kong won, making it an even situation. The outcome will not be known until tomorrow. The results of yesterday are recorded below:

Men's Group

Xiao Xu's Skills Still Need Improvement

The competition started at 1:30 PM. Qiu Feihai replaced Lin Baohua. Old Qiu has gradually recovered his original form recently, but his physical strength is still not as good as before. Xu is a rising star in Hong Kong and his skills are above Li Huitang. He was placed in the third singles to avoid the complete defeat of Hong Kong. Unexpectedly, Qiu still defeated him yesterday. At this time, Carlson knew that he could not be casual anymore, and with a little more effort, he ended with 6-2. When the match was over, dusk had already gathered, and it was time to turn on the lights. He and Hong can be proud of this achievement.

Sino-Japanese Baseball Friendly Match; Shanghai City Team Suffers a Crushing Defeat; Mr. Li Zeyi is Invited to Throw the First Pitch; Total Score: 12 to 3, Shanghai Textile Wins 151

The Shanghai baseball team, the city's representative in the All-China Games, played a Sino-Japanese friendship friendly match with the Japanese Shangfang Textile Company at the Shangfang Association ball field on Linqing Road yesterday afternoon. The match began at 2:35 PM. Mr. Li Zeyi, a government advisor known for his integrity, was specially invited to throw the first pitch. The game ended at 4:40 PM, with Shangfang winning 12 to 3. After the game, a tea party was held at the venue, and everyone dispersed happily.

Match Situation

At 2:35 PM, after Mr. Li Zeyi threw the first pitch, the Shanghai team took the offensive first. Zeng Ruiqi got a hit and scored the first point. The Shangfang team failed, and the Shanghai team took the lead with a score of 1 to 0. In the second inning, Shanghai achieved nothing, and Shangfang scored two consecutive hits, reversing the situation with a score of 5 to 1. In the third and fourth innings, neither side gained anything. In the fifth inning, Shangfang scored four consecutive points. The Shanghai team cheered up and, in the sixth inning, Liang Fuchu and Liang Chengsong each returned to home base, adding two more points. In the seventh inning, both sides maintained their chastity. In the eighth inning, Shangfang's Gao Song hit a ground ball that landed on the first base line and rolled away. The left fielder failed to catch it, and three players from Shangfang returned to home base, adding another three points. In the final inning, three players from the Shanghai team were already on base, and Yang Huayuan had a heavy responsibility. However, his luck was bad, and he failed, ending the game with a score of 3 to 12.

Overall Assessment of Skills

Overall, the skills of both sides were evenly matched. The Shanghai team's pitcher, Gan Cheng, and catcher, Gan Ruikang, and the Shangfang team's pitchers, Heiyan and Yongsong, and catcher, Mizumatsu, were all at a high level. Although neither side made any special contributions yesterday, their sharp and elusive skills were already quite advanced. The three-tier personnel were also quite well-balanced. However, the Shanghai team's outfield was too weak, missing nine out of ten high balls. For example, Gao Song's ground ball in the eighth inning was quite easy to catch, but it slipped through the fielder's legs, which was a great loss. Otherwise, only one more person from Shangfang could have returned to home base in that inning. Therefore, the reason for yesterday's defeat was that there were too many errors in the outfield. According to the hit records, Shangfang scored more points, but they had nine hits, while Shanghai also had five hits. Moreover, Zeng Ying once had a triple and Zeng Ruiqi once had a double. Shangfang only Mizumatsu had a double. This proves that the offensive power was still strong. However, the Shangfang factory is one of the local strong teams, and baseball is the national sport of the Japanese, so Shanghai's attack is not surprising. Therefore, the hope of winning the championship at the All-China Games is very high.

The Course of Rent Disputes at Peiping Republic College 162

(Nanjing, 29th) Regarding the rent dispute at Peiping Republic College, the person in charge of the school said that the school building was originally the residence of Prince Chun of the Qing Dynasty. When it was leased eleven years ago, a contract was signed stating that the monthly rent was 200 yuan. After paying for one month, the payment was discontinued because the property was to be used for public purposes. After the Mukden Incident, when Prince Chun went to the puppet state, he entrusted a Japanese person to demand 25,000 yuan in unpaid rent over the past eleven years. Lu Dangping has already presented the details of the matter to Minister Wang of the Ministry of Education and requested instructions on how to handle it. For the time being, he will not go to Peiping.

Recent Educational News from Anhui Province 163

The following is a brief summary of the recent educational situation in Anhui Province:

(A) Elementary Education (1) "Planning for Universal Education in the Provincial Capital": The total number of out-of-school adults and children in the provincial capital has been surveyed last year. Since the adoption of various implementation measures by the Universal Education Committee, the implementation of universal education in the provincial capital has started in April and will be completed within one year. Methods such as the teaching-student service method, two-part system, short-term primary school classes, universal education classes, and universal education groups are adopted and promoted separately. It starts with persuasion, and those who do not comply with persuasion will be forced by law. Four volumes of universal education readers have been compiled, and it is stipulated that those receiving education should complete these readers and understand their meaning as the standard. The responsibility for promotion is undertaken by the provincial elementary schools in each district. (2) "Establishment of a Central Science Experiment Room for Primary Schools in the Provincial Capital": In order to enrich the scientific equipment of primary schools in the provincial capital and increase the efficiency of science teaching, the Department of Education has established a central science experiment room for primary schools in the provincial capital. The provincial primary schools in the provincial capital are planned to be divided into four districts, with one central science experiment room set up in each district, and a Science Education Committee is organized to be responsible for managing the experiment rooms and planning and guiding science teaching in each school. The Department of Education will purchase physics and chemistry instruments, medicines, and biological models and specimens and distribute them to each experiment room to facilitate teaching.

(B) Secondary Education (1) "Revising the Regulations for Teacher Training Students' Observation and Practice": In accordance with the regulations for teacher training schools promulgated by the Ministry, the Department of Education has recently revised the regulations for teacher training students' observation and travel that were formulated last year, in order to better suit the actual situation, and has issued them to all schools for compliance. (2) "Vocational School Graduates Are Not Allowed to Participate in Observation and Travel": In the past, vocational school students in the province used to have observation and travel activities in their last semester. Now, in accordance with the regulations, emphasis is placed on practical training, and all vocational schools are ordered not to follow the example of teacher training students in conducting observation and travel. All vocational schools have complied with this and will not conduct observation and travel this semester.

(C) Higher Education "Holding Examinations for Government-Funded Students to Study in Europe": The province selected and sent two government-funded students majoring in hydraulic engineering, one in electrical engineering, one in civil engineering, and two in crop breeding to study in Europe last summer. Because there are still vacancies for government-funded students to study in Europe, the Department of Education, in order to cultivate talents, held another examination this year in July to send three government-funded students to study in Europe, including one in mechanical engineering in countries such as England, Germany, France, and Belgium, one in mining and metallurgy in Germany, and one in agriculture in Germany, Denmark, and other countries.

(D) Social Education "Issuing Standards for Compiling Social Education Expenditure Estimates": The Department of Education stipulated that social education expenditure should account for a certain percentage of the total education expenditure, ranging from 10% to 20%, when instructed by the Ministry of Education, and ordered all counties to comply. In the 23rd year of the Republic, there were still many counties where the social education expenditure was far from the prescribed percentage. In order to expand the social education expenditure in each county, the Department of Education has specially formulated the standards and precautions for the social education expenditure to be compiled by each county in the 24th year of the Republic, and ordered all counties to pay special attention to compliance.

Local Education (1) "Abolishing Education Bureaus and Establishing Sections": In order to improve the efficiency of local education administration, the province has temporarily designated several counties to try abolishing the county education bureaus and establishing education sections attached to the county government. County education administrative matters are carried out in the name of the county magistrate. The county magistrate is responsible for education funding and must ensure its independence and maintenance. Under no circumstances shall it be misappropriated. The county magistrate is also responsible for increasing revenue, improving old debts and new credits. The county's education funding is managed by an education funding management committee. The original education funding committee is changed to an education funding audit committee. (2) "Custody of Education Funds in Chuzhou County": In order to manage the entire county's education fund, Anhui Province’s Chuzhou County organized the Chuzhou County Education Fund Management Committee, which is responsible for custody and auditing. This fund should account for 2% to 5% of the total county educational expenditure. The specific percentage for each year is determined by the committee. The education fund cannot be used except for one of the following circumstances: (1) Temporarily borrowing funds for essential maintenance when there is a shortage; (3) Allocating funds to maintain the status quo due to disaster and poor harvest. The education fund passbook is kept by the Education Special Fund Committee, and its seal is kept by the Chairman of the Committee for mutual supervision.

Little Men (6) (1) 168

— Originally Written by Ms. Alcott of the United States, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

"They won't know, Uncle Bay is not home, Mrs. Bay is busy taking care of Tandy; he has something like a throat ailment, she can't leave him for a step, we won't sit up until late at night, and there won't be any noise, what else is preventing us?"

"If we leave the lamp on for too long, Assy will know, she always notices when it's like this."

"No, she won't, I've prepared a dark lantern for this; it won't let out much light, and we can turn it off immediately when we hear someone coming," said Don, and Ned was moved by this idea, thinking that new life was delightful. He immediately went out to inform Tomo, but then stuck his head back in and said:

"You want Little Bridge too, don't you?"

"No, I don't; if you tell that moralist, he'll stick up two crow's eyes at you, and they're already asleep, so just glance at Tomo and come back immediately."

Ned followed his words and came back in a moment, followed by Tomo, who was only wearing one piece of clothing, his hair disheveled, and drowsy, but just like his behavior, he was prepared to come and have fun together.

"Now don't be hungry, I'll teach you how to play a wonderful game called 'Poker'," said Don, at which time the three young men who knew how to have fun were already sitting around the table, on which were placed a bottle, cigars and playing cards, "Let's drink a little first, then everyone will hold a 'Weed' and play poker together, this is what adults do, it's really fun." (Note 2)

(Note 2) "Weed" is used to translate Cigar smoke and so on.

Free Talk

Superfluous Words 169

— Yu

Let me say a few words as usual. It seems to be superfluous. A thing itself has a certain limited value. It does not need an individual's subjective, overly high or low evaluation to affirm or deny its existence. In fact, it is inevitable to fall into error to think that this partial selection is sufficient to represent everything, or insufficient to represent everything. We cannot affirm everything because of our likes and dislikes, just as we cannot deny everything because of our likes and dislikes. However, we must understand this point, that is: a thing attains the highest evaluation from society due to its objective existence, which is definitely not the advocacy of a few people, but due to the needs of the majority. Those who consider themselves masters of ××, or the founders of ××, obliterate the entire process of the occurrence of a thing—both its beginning and its development—and attribute it to the power of individuals. This is inevitable to place so much emphasis on the small ego, which is not very important, while neglecting the great ego outside oneself. This is because those who are ignorant of reality account for five out of ten, and those who are subjectively arrogant account for five out of ten. If individuals are calm and peaceful, get rid of their arrogance, and observe the actual situation clearly, they will understand that the power of individuals is truly insignificant. Once we understand this point, then we can understand that the recent development of essays—or what some people call miscellanies—is not the result of the advocacy of a particular person or a particular group, but there are objective conditions for its development. That is, the changes in modern economic institutions and the development of mechanical civilization have made everyone's daily life proceed at a high speed. People involved in this vortex, except for friends who live in pavilions, use literature as a tool for eating, or those leisurely classes who want to claim to be erudite and still read long and thick novels, most citizens no longer have such leisure. In this way, short, powerful, and stimulating essays will naturally become the best spiritual food for the general public. The development of essays is then the inevitable result.

Speaking of this, some people may raise objections, thinking that this situation may be true in Europe and the United States, but not necessarily in China. Chinese people have plenty of free time. In the inland areas, you can see that playing a game of mahjong will take up an entire morning, drinking a glass of wine will take up half a day, and drinking a pot of tea will take up an entire afternoon, and smoking a few pipes of opium will consume an entire lifetime. You can see laziness and slowness everywhere. Walking like ants crawling, doing things like lazy cattle proceeding. You may ask where is the high speed? Where is the tense life? However, if you take a look at the metropolis that came in with the Western cannons and the cities affected by it, you may get a clear impression. At the corners of the asphalt roads in the morning and evening, you can see that in the middle of the road, vehicles are galloping like the wind, and people are surging like a tide. A dynamic - high-speed moving city is displayed in front of you, and the people in this city, although not necessarily all living a high-speed life, the rhythm of this high speed is affecting their heads to some extent. With such a lifestyle, and with a part of the people in this lifestyle, social institutions that are suitable for this lifestyle naturally also occur. Naturally, in the city, there are special organizations for these people to consume, special entertainment venues for these people to consume, and naturally, at the same time, there must also be special spiritual food to supply these people. Yellow newspapers, "mosquito newspapers" are one kind, humorous magazines and picture magazines are another kind, and more pure magazines and newspapers are another kind. Under such circumstances, the so-called soft article has developed unprecedentedly.

Speaking of the special development of small magazines carrying so-called essays in China in recent years, there is another special reason for investigating its actual situation, that is, on the one hand, because the contradictions in society are becoming increasingly profound, and grasping this phenomenon, the poisonous satirical literature has become particularly prosperous, and the passive ones only "entrust sadness to humor," while the active ones naturally have a kind of edifying meaning in them. On the other hand, because of the increasing economic depression of the nation and the shrinking purchasing power of the people, buying more expensive books has become the right of special classes and is no longer within the ability of ordinary people, and no one cares about newly published books, and magazines with lower prices have become the target of mass purchases, which is an inevitable result, and the sudden rise of the magazine industry is not without reason.

Whether such a phenomenon is good or bad is another question, which is not within the scope of this article's discussion, but the development of essays has its own value and will never be as worthless as ordinary people scold. Similarly, the development of essays is definitely not an obstacle to the production of great works. Although we admit that the era of "Tyranny of Fiction" has passed, we cannot admit that the development of essays is the result of the exhaustion of novel themes. Koizumi Yakumo talked about this opinion decades ago. Koizumi Yakumo believes that European novels in the past two hundred years, with love as the theme, have almost exhausted all kinds of themes and forms, and future novels must find a new way. What is the new way of novels? He did not tell us, but he told us that prose (Essay) and sketch (Sketch) will definitely occupy an important position in literature in the future. Although triangular love and quadrilateral love novels have flourished for a while in China in the past few years, these novels are not enough to represent everything, and they have not exhausted the themes. Chinese novels seem to have a common new trend in the future, with a promising future, and the development of essays is actually going on in parallel. There is no need for me to defend the essays. In the near future, the facts will tell us.

Of course, in terms of these two natures, the writing of essays is lighter in weight, easier to write, and more free in form. The death of an old woman next door can be used as the subject matter of an essay, and a car crushing a small dog can also be used as the subject matter of an essay; essays can write about the vastness of the universe or the insignificance of flies. However, what essays are different from novels is that you only need to describe the outline of a thing with the simplest pen, which is enough. You don't need to write about half a day of a person's life with hundreds of pages of words like a novel. Just like modern cartoons, you only need to use a few strokes to depict the characteristics of a person or event vividly on paper to exhaust its function. Therefore, if you want to draw a Cyrano, you only need to draw a big nose. If you want to draw the absurd actions of the mad knight Don Quixote, you only need to draw a knight riding a skinny horse to fight windmills. If you want to draw Chaplin, you only need to draw a pair of big leather shoes or draw a cane or draw a small beard. If you want to draw Joan Crawford, you only need to draw a pair of big eyes, which is enough. I believe that those who can grasp this point will definitely be able to write a good essay, and I believe that those who ignore this point will definitely be struggling to no avail. My standard of selection is like this. Whether there are subjective errors in it is naturally open to discussion, and whether what I have selected meets this standard is naturally difficult to say.

Home 170

— Menghua

Every night, after I get rid of all my duties, I walk out of the store with "body fatigue". I'm used to the dim yellow electric lights, and when I leave the store, I feel a little dizzy. I can't hear the noisy city sounds, I can't see the beautiful night street scene, I'm blank, as lonely as if I'm in a desert. I just anxiously drag this tired body into an alley, and then wipe past a few, turning, and walking towards my home.

I stopped outside a house with peeling paint, this is my home. I quietly knocked on the door a few times, and the old landlord came to answer the sound. The door opened, and I answered the landlord's greetings while hurrying in, opening my own room door, twisting the electric light, and sitting blankly on the chair as before.

At this time, I began the silent thought of home.

"Is this my home?" I asked myself this as if I were practicing old habits. Yes, I still have only one home, and I have been away from it for almost ten years. But once I leave it. I never think of it at any time, and what revolves in my mind is a new, future home, a happy and gentle home. There I can completely recover from the fatigue of the day and not feel any disgust or boredom.

"This is not the request of a selfish person, nor is it the concept of a vulgar person, even a chicken has a perch, a dog has a nest, how can a person not have a home?" I often reasoned with myself like this. So I sank again into my ocean of ideals, this ocean of our future ideals. In this way, I felt as if I was immersed in the warm spring sun, lying on the soft, grassy fields, and I felt the preciousness of life and the comfort of living.

However, the home where I sit by the window is a house that is both leaky and dirty. There are piles of stove ashes outside the house, and there are piles of stove ashes inside the house. There is a thick, thin layer of ashes sprinkled on the table, the desk, the bookshelf, and the bed. The light is so dim, and people are so tired. Seeing and hearing these things, I fell out of the circle of ideals in disappointment and resentment. I heard the rumbling of the trams in the up and down, the cries of those sad peddlers floating in the sea of people, as well as the cough of the landlord's chronic lung disease.

I am, and my thoughts turn to another dark alley.

"Don't I also have a mother who coughs like this all day long?" I thought. Yes, I have heard people say that. Because when I had just touched the sunlight, my mother had left me forever. In my memory, Dad's impression is also blurred, as if he was a tall, black and thin man, because he left me when I could walk, and went to other places to leave his dilapidated and unrecognizable home. So I was raised by an aunt who was cruel and vented her private anger by whipping other people's children. When I could just walk (naturally, this is a social path), I was determined and learned from my dad and ran away. For ten years, I was a homeless person. He ran away for an ideal, that was very clear, and his child also left the so-called home for an ideal, that was also very clear. But until now, none of us know where anyone is going, maybe he ended his life for that ideal? My poor dad.

The sound from the landlord came over again when my thoughts were interrupted, and therefore I felt even more sad.

A Story of Pigeons 171

— Ling He

I spent the entire summer relaxing with the children in the countryside.

Being in the countryside, I was far away from my friends. As a result, most of them had forgotten about me, and the manuscript deadlines weren't as pressing as before, so I felt much more at ease. Aside from sharing in the children's laughter and joy, I also became quite interested in the daily lives of the host's pigeons.

There were four pigeons in total, and the host housed them in two separate rooms. As the host told me, they were two married couples. The couple upstairs hadn't had any offspring, while the downstairs couple had already had a little one. Amidst the busyness of people's trivial lives, one could hear the little life chirping incessantly, a cry of hunger awaiting feeding. So the mother busied herself feeding the baby, taking turns with the father. Day after day passed, and slowly, one could see the little pigeon growing scattered, stiff feathers. It seemed their lives, though busy, were also peaceful and happy.

Pigeons, in the eyes of artists, are regarded as symbols of peace. At this time, I also understood that pigeons were indeed lovely.

One morning, before dawn had fully broken, I, fond of the coolness of summer mornings, got up by myself. Opening the front door, a sweet, cool breeze rushed towards me, making me feel as if my chest had suddenly expanded a lot. The bamboo leaves in the courtyard were covered in pearl-like morning dew, reluctant to fall. I deliberately walked back and forth barefoot on the grass, my feet thoroughly cleansed by the dew. In this setting, I deeply understood the loveliness of summer.

Suddenly, a loud whistling sound rang above my head, which also gave one a sense of clarity. It turned out to be a flock of pigeons flying by. Who knew that misfortune would begin from here? When eating lunch that day, I was the first to notice that the mother pigeon had flown away, as she wasn't there picking up rice grains by the table. All the way until dusk, it was clear that the little pigeon's mother wasn't coming back. Gone, gone, perhaps never to fly back to her husband and child. The hostess complained, saying:

"It's that Zhang family's big house, they really don't do good deeds. Every morning, they release their pigeons, making them coo and coo, attracting other people's pigeons. I bought this pair for two hundred coppers, and now one has gone, what a pity!"

I didn't dare misquote a single word of what the hostess said. After all, half of the two hundred coppers had flown away, so it was understandable that she felt pained. Moreover, I had long known that she wanted pigeons because her daughter-in-law hadn't given her any grandchildren after more than three years of marriage. After consulting with Old Lin the doctor, she was told that she needed to nourish her yin, so she bought four pigeons in two batches. She had personally told her daughter-in-law that once the little pigeons had two pairs, then she would kill the big ones for her daughter-in-law to eat alone. A mother-in-law treating her daughter-in-law with such great kindness was truly rare in the world. Not long ago, one little one hatched, which really made the hostess happy. However, now that one was born and one was lost, one canceling out the other, there was still no additional one. Naturally! Perhaps it really was her daughter-in-law's bad luck. And the mother-in-law's blaming heaven and earth had its own reasons.

I don't know if pigeons also understand the sorrow of lost love, but I did see that the widowed male pigeon was truly uneasy for two or three days. One moment it would fly to the roof and coo, the next it would coo beside the nest. The feathers on its neck were stretched out as much as possible, but aside from the motherless child chirping and begging its father for food, no wife paid it any attention. And the couple upstairs simply looked at it freely, seemingly without resentment or sympathy.

Based on my imagination, the Zhang family's big house must be a magnificent, resplendent mansion. Then the pigeon coop must also be luxurious and splendid. Of course, the pigeons' food there must be very good, so every male would have extremely beautiful plumage. In the mornings with gentle breezes, they would happily soar into the sky. With the bells tied to their feet by the owner, emitting loud sounds that resonated in the sky, how envious their fellow pigeons must be! So this young mother, breaking free from the troublesome life of raising children, leaving her simple husband, following them to the Zhang family's big house to enjoy herself, what's so unreasonable about that?

I don't know why, but perhaps the hatred in the world hadn't completely worn away my sympathy, and I was very concerned about that pigeon. Since losing its wife, I saw that it was even more diligent in feeding its child. It would open its beak, letting the child forcefully peck at its throat to get rice grains. It endured the pain, constantly moving backwards, while the child pressed tightly, drilling deep into its throat. Naturally, this was an unavoidable obligation for it: to feed its own child, carefully watching over it as it slowly grew up. Its wife could shirk this responsibility, but it couldn't! Could it also bear to fly far away, leaving its child to starve to death?

It flew outside several times each day. Perhaps it was looking for its wife, which would forever disappoint it. Otherwise, it was going outside to look for food. Indeed, the hostess sometimes generously scattered a few grains of broken rice on the ground for the pigeons, but that was so little that it could be counted. And the couple upstairs desperately fought to peck at it. No matter how quick its beak movements were, it was ultimately just a matter of evenly splitting the food. But its share had to feed itself and its child. But with its meager strength, in this desolate and cruel world, how much leftover food from humans could it find?

Like every animal's fondness for its own offspring, this poor father truly did his best to care for his child. It used its beak to scratch the child, comb its feathers, and peck away the gradually falling down. Seeing the shiny, black new feathers gradually growing on the child, how intense its joy must be.

Originally, this was also a very natural thing, feeling especially sorry for a child who has lost its mother, and caring for it doubly; perhaps this pigeon also had the same inspiration as humans, so when the male pigeon upstairs flew near its nest or stood at the entrance for a while, it would fight it with all its might, to defend it from harming its child, until it left. But when the female one upstairs came near, it didn't hit it, but rather cooed, expressing amorous frivolity, as if treating it like its lost wife. This might be a sexual reaction, but the female one ignored it and walked away, which was inevitably an embarrassing insult. Precisely because of this, it hated the male one even more, and several times I saw them fighting for no reason, falling from the high pigeon coop, feathers torn and scattered, and blood flowing.

I often thought this: even the god of peace fights, no wonder human wars are such natural behaviors, although they are also very terrible.

The child grew bigger day by day. Covered in shiny feathers, it could actually fly from the coop to the ground. But at this time, the father lost the hair on its head. The child's feathers were full, but it won itself a bald head. I selfishly pondered silently. Who was this ultimately for? It wasn't until I learned from others that the newly grown child was its daughter that I realized it was actually placing great hopes on its daughter. Later, I indeed saw it several times following behind its daughter, cooing like it did to the female one upstairs, but the daughter coldly avoided it every time. No, if the daughter didn't disappoint her, then its bald head wouldn't be without a price. I silently prayed for its wish to succeed.

The summer vacation passed, and I quietly returned to where I originally lived. Nearly two months in the countryside ultimately left me with a lot of memories, and the pitiful pigeon, as Hui Ru said, was also something I sometimes thought about. A letter from the countryside told me that the newly grown female pigeon had, like its mother, also flown away to an unknown place. I didn't know if I should worry about the male pigeon, but its pitiful bald head flashed in my mind several times.

The Responsibility of Beauty (I) 172

— Original by George Bernard Shaw (Translated by Ding)

In the private office of a law firm, a litigant paced back and forth. They were both young men. The litigant said:

——No, Schatto: This separation case. I'm going to settle it right away.

——Listen to me, Hollis.

——I don't want to listen to you. Nor do I want to listen to anyone. My wife and I only have divorce as an option.

——But, my dear Hollis, you have nothing against her.

——Nothing against her…

——I'm telling you, since you have nothing against her. Then you shouldn't criticize her character, her housekeeping, and all the other things; except that she makes you jealous.

——I'm not jealous, but I can't avoid this emotion, so I should have a reason.

——Then, Hollis. If you separate from her based on this reason, then you already have grounds for divorce.

——I'm absolutely willing to divorce—I mean I want to divorce her. But you always tell me it's not possible.

——It's all not possible. You're not accusing her of the kind of wrongful conduct: just accusing her with words. Words aren't of much use.

——You still think it's not bad enough. This shows how ignorant you are about the affair. The lawyer couldn't bear it anymore and said:

——Hey, fine. Then do it your own way. What do you want to sue for now?

——What are you planning to do?

——Me! What? Old man, I'll drag your wife here today and tell her you've decided to separate from her. Do you think I'll do something like this without giving her a reason?

——I might as well tell you: No one else can tolerate it.

Fleeing the Famine 174

— Jia Chengsheng

When a year of famine is encountered, and there is no harvest in the fields, farmers lose their livelihood. Driven by hunger and cold, and having no other choice, they apply to the local government for a passport. They travel in groups, supporting the old and leading the young, fleeing to other places to find food. This is called "fleeing the famine."

"Fleeing the famine" is originally something done out of necessity under circumstances where there is no other option. However, things happen unexpectedly, and there are even those who take "fleeing the famine" as a regular occupation. This is truly what is called a strange custom.

In Funing County, Jiangsu, there are several places where the folk customs are very fierce. They are accustomed to a life where, every year after the autumn harvest, when the farming season is over, regardless of whether the year is abundant or lean, the entire village unites and goes to the county to apply for a passport. Every family abandons the joy of home and becomes a "famine refugee" who leaves their hometown. From autumn to winter, they wander in other places, living their nomadic lives, until the next year when the spring is warm and the flowers are fragrant, when everyone returns and goes back to cultivate their own fields.

For example, if there is a family in this village who feels that their harvest is sufficient for their livelihood and is unwilling to go outside to "flee the famine" with them, that is not allowed. Then, everyone in the village will first come to your house to eat, eating everything you have until it is completely gone. In the end, you still have to go "fleeing the famine" with them. Therefore, farmers who have a little bit of food have long since moved away.

Every year during the autumn harvest season, the Funing County government routinely prepares a certain number of passports, waiting for them to request them. It has almost become a formulaic task. The government has no way to stop this strange custom, otherwise, if they don't go out to "flee the famine," they will cause trouble in the local area.

A Record of Rock Piling in Guyi Garden, Nanxiang 175

— Haiyang Yuyin

Since ancient times, the best scenery in famous gardens has been trees and rocks, and the rise and fall of fortune also depends on trees and rocks. Lush trees are a sign of prosperity; dilapidated rocks are a sign of decline. Rocks are the natural essence of heaven and earth, called cloud roots. Rocks with essence are called spiritual rocks, and rocks without essence are called stubborn rocks. In the past, Shengong lectured on the Dharma, and stubborn rocks nodded. Chuping attained enlightenment and scolded rocks to become sheep. It can be seen that rocks do have spiritual essence. During the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty, Ye rebuilt Guyi Garden and piled up artificial mountains such as Douyun Cave, the Five Elders Peak, and the Eighteen Scholars, which were quite spectacular. During the Red Sheep Calamity in the Xianfeng and Tongzhi period, they were already destroyed. During the January 28th Incident, they were further ravaged. Visitors to the garden deeply regretted this. Chuan Zuohong, a gentleman from Puzuo, saw this and hired a Jinhua technician to estimate the cost of repairs. Li Liangcai tried his best to raise funds, and noble gentlemen generously donated. Construction began in mid-July of the year Yihai and was completed in early August. The Douyun Cave has steps that can be climbed, winding into the cave. Mr. Dai Cangyan inscribed "Little Tiantai," and the Eighteen Scholars, Five Elders Peak, and Wanjuanshu Rock were restored to their former appearance. They are even more majestic and magnificent. Su Shi of Meishan said: The rise and fall, prosperity and destruction of things cannot be known. Today's beautiful trees and spiritual rocks, how long will it be before they are buried in desolate smoke and weeds? It is also impossible to know. However, with those who fall forward being followed by those who rise up behind, never changing, although they have gone through ancient times, they are like new. May this garden be immortal.

Disaster victims are here for sightseeing, not for disaster relief!

Watching the Tide Under the Moon 176

— (Sun Linchang)

The tide of Haining is a marvel that shocks China and the world. The time of the tide is relative to noon and midnight, so if there is a daytime tide, there must be a nighttime tide, and the nighttime tide is often more magnificent than the daytime tide. However, people only value daytime viewing and rarely watch at night. Little do they know that at midnight, "the moon hangs in the sky, the waves are calm and silent, and the flowing water swallows the light of the moon," which is a unique spectacle. Before long, the wind turns cold, and the sea gate rises with the tide. The moonlight and waves spray snow from afar, the clouds move the jade shore, and the waves roll with the sound of thunder, like a white silk sail rising in the wind, flying and twisting, with the force of breaking bamboo. The ancients said: "The sound of a hundred thousand troops is like the midnight tide," truly so. Watching the night tide is even more spectacular because the bright moonlight reflects the surging snow waves. However, the construction of the Haining coast is very rudimentary. Although people have the refined interest of watching the night tide, they have to retreat due to the lack of lodging. It is now said that the Hangzhou Provincial Highway Bureau, in view of this, has specially set up a temporary hostel by the river, located on the seawall, facing the river tide, with a particularly novel arrangement, for people who watch the night tide to linger.

Records of Lingering Fragrance 178

— Originally written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

In the past, wealthy families were always very particular about drinking tea. The best tea leaves had to be bought for one or two taels of silver per pound, which was indeed a luxury. Because it was a luxury, our Empress Dowager particularly enjoyed using it. Whether the tea she drank was really better than all the others, I dare not say, I only know that their prices were very alarming, at least one or two taels of silver could buy one or two catties. Every time the Empress Dowager drank tea, she had to change the tea leaves, and she also liked to mix various dried flowers, such as roses and jasmine, with the tea leaves and brew them together, taking their fragrance. Among them, wild lilyturf flowers were particularly praised by the Empress Dowager. There were almost always a few wild lilyturf flowers floating in her teacup every time she drank.

Lotus petals were also something the Empress Dowager loved to eat. In the summer, the imperial kitchen was often instructed to pick many fresh lotus flowers, take the most intact petals, soak them in flour mixed with chicken eggs, divide them into sweet and salty, add some chicken broth or refined sugar, and fry them in a wok until golden brown, making a very palatable snack. Also, in the spring, around the time of the Qingming Festival, when the tall magnolia flowers were in full bloom, the Empress Dowager would also have them picked, and following the method of using lotus flowers, fry them into fragrant, sweet, and crispy magnolia slices, eating them at any time to pass the time.

Since there were so many flowers and trees planted in the imperial garden, and each flower and tree had to be taken care of at all times, the work of the eunuchs who served as gardeners for the Empress Dowager was really very arduous! Just taking chrysanthemums as an example, they are only seasonal flowers, and only need to be taken care of in the autumn. Although we have a large greenhouse to cover them, and we can keep them until winter, most of the time that they need to be taken care of is in the autumn. It seems like it shouldn't be too busy. World News

The Protector of Royalty 179

— Blue

The emperors or leaders of various countries in the world are often the center of attention. Wherever they go, thousands of eyes are fixed upon them, as if they were the target of public criticism. In continental Europe, whenever emperors or crown princes travel, they are always surrounded by numerous military police, detectives, and plainclothes detectives, who protect them at all times and in all places, otherwise they would be suspicious and unable to move an inch. If they attend any public ceremony, it is even more tense, as if every step is fraught with thorns and every place is full of danger. However, royalty in England enjoys great freedom. Even if emperors of other countries, due to revolutionary upheavals in their own nations, flee in disgrace and are pursued by political assassins, they often regard England as their only haven of peace and happiness. For example, after the abdication of the former King Alfonso of Spain, he also lived as a foreign resident in England. He could openly watch horse races or play ball games in restaurants, enjoying such freedom and ease. He felt that there was no safer place in the world than England.

However, unexpected events may occur, so British detectives also do their best to protect royalty. The world-famous Scotland Yard has a special section dedicated to protecting royalty or leaders such as presidents from other countries. Whenever these state guests step off the train at Victoria Station, Scotland Yard detectives secretly follow them.

The royalty of England do not need protection. They can come and go as they please, without fear of any danger, because they are all loved by the people. People often see young princes going to the cinema to watch movies, dining in restaurants, or spending their leisure time in public dance halls, pleasures that princes on the continent cannot enjoy. As soon as they leave the palace gates, they are always escorted by troops and followed closely by military officers, as if they were being escorted as criminals.

The princes of England are not only unguarded in their own country, but they are also casual and carefree when they go abroad, without fear of unexpected attacks. Once, Duke Grosvenor, the prince, took a mail ship to Eton. There were many Indians among the passengers on board, who were very noisy. At that time, the ship received a wireless message stating that there had been a major strike and boycott of British goods in Bombay, India, which had led to clashes with the police. Upon hearing this news, the Indian youths on board were filled with excitement. However, the Duke remained calm and strolled on the deck, swam in the swimming pool, or played various games, without any worries. He did not even guard against an attack by the Indians.

During the unstable period in Egypt, assassins roamed everywhere, but the eldest prince of Wales, the British heir, calmly paraded through the streets of Cairo. He did not carry any weapons for self-defense, only a golf club.

Of course, covert protection is indispensable. Whenever the Prince of Wales mingles with ordinary people, there is often a broad-shouldered and powerful man following him from a distance, fulfilling his responsibility to protect him. This man's name is White, formerly a famous detective at Scotland Yard, who is also famous for protecting royalty. White is always loyal to the Prince of Wales, never slacking. Wherever the prince goes, he goes, truly like his shadow, and his comings and goings are elusive, with a mysterious meaning. The prince has used various methods to test White's skills, which are indeed as sharp as a police dog. The prince always talks about it with great relish when he is with his brothers.

Whenever the prince goes to the cinema to watch a movie, White is always in the back row of seats. If the prince finishes his last cigarette, White will come up and offer him a pack of his favorite cigarettes. If the prince goes down a coal mine, to the darkest depths, White has already brought a lantern and caught up. If the prince goes to the St. Andrews golf course, White is already there waiting with a golf club. The prince has tried everything to get rid of White, but rarely succeeds.

Even if the prince uses flight as a method, he cannot escape White. He has already received the news and taken another plane first. When the prince steps down from his plane, it is White who is holding his arm at the door. White's two broad shoulders almost bear the safety of the prince's entire body.
