Economic Supplement

The Tax Burden of the Chinese People 180

— (Zhao Chaogou)

I. The People's Ability to Bear Taxes

To make up for a country's financial shortfall, there are only two options: (1) issuing public debt, and (2) increasing taxes. When public debt reaches its limit, the focus turns to increasing taxes. However, increasing taxes results in increasing the burden on the people. Therefore, regardless of whether the tax system is good or bad, it is necessary to examine whether the people have the ability to pay taxes. If the people's burden has already reached its maximum limit, increasing taxes becomes even more dangerous. Historically, the core of tax discussion has been (1) how far can taxes be increased, and (2) can the people bear the maximum level of taxation. In the past, there was a school of optimistic heavy tax proponents who believed that only heavy taxes could lead the country to prosperity. There was also a school of thought on currency circulation, which believed that taxes were merely a reduction in currency circulation and would not cause much sacrifice to the people. However, neither of these theories has gained general sympathy. Based on common sense, the theory of light taxes is more likely to resonate with the general public. However, blindly believing in the theory of light taxes is also dangerous. The more a country evolves, the more diverse the duties borne by the government, and its expenditure naturally gradually expands. Without adequate income, how can the government fulfill its duties? Therefore, modern economists neither advocate the heavy tax theory, which speaks from the government's point of view, nor the populist and family-pleasing total tax theory. They all have a consensus: to determine the amount of taxes the country levies on the people based on the people's ability to pay taxes. The attention of financial economists to taxation theory is based on this fair concept. For example, after the end of the European War, the Allied Reparations Committee, when deciding on the total amount of German reparations, examined the German tax system and compared the burden on the German people with the burden on the Allied people to determine Germany's ability to pay reparations.

II. National Wealth, Income, and Tax-Bearing Capacity

National wealth and national income are mostly hypothetical figures, and naturally cannot be considered precise. However, on the whole, they are still a standard for measuring the people's ability to bear burdens. According to the economic principles of taxation, the amount of taxes that a country levies on its people must never erode national wealth, but can only be taken from national income. Therefore, national wealth and national income are of great importance to the ability to bear taxes. In the tax systems of modern countries, both property tax and income tax are listed. These two taxes both take property and income as the direct objects of taxation, and the amount of tax is directly determined by the amount of national wealth and national income. In essence, all taxes are, in a broad sense, income taxes, because no matter what kind of tax is collected, it is all drawn from the people's income. Therefore, to measure the people's ability to bear burdens, national income can be used as a direct standard, and national wealth as an indirect standard. The following is a list of the national wealth of various countries for comparison with China's national wealth. (The unit of the numbers in the table below is million Japanese yen for the top row, and Japanese yen per capita for the bottom row.)

Comparison of National Wealth of Various Countries

National Wealth Average Wealth

per Capita

United States 762,356 6,707

United Kingdom 136,320 5,147

France 103,320 2,549

Japan 102,353 1,721

National Wealth Average Wealth

per Capita

Germany 71,685 1,141

Italy 44,786 1,027

China 38,296 90

The above table is copied from "A List of National Conditions of Various Countries" published by the Japan Cabinet Statistics Bureau. The figure for China's national wealth is noted as being from a 1922 survey. Looking at this table, the difference between China and the major powers in national wealth is astounding. The average wealth per capita is more than 73 times less than that of the United States, more than 59 times less than that of the United Kingdom, and even nearly 20 times less than that of its eastern neighbor, Japan. The ability of the Chinese people to bear taxes can also be compared with that of other countries in proportion to this difference in magnitude. In other words, if the Japanese people can only bear 20 yuan in taxes per year, then the Chinese people can only bear 2 yuan per year, and the American people can bear 40 yuan. This certainly cannot be taken as an exact proportion, but it can give a glimpse of the weakness of the Chinese people's ability to bear taxes.

The weakness of the Chinese people's ability to bear burdens can also be seen by comparing their average national income with their tax burden.

Comparison of Average Income of People in Various Countries

The figure for the average income of the Chinese people, although an estimate by the Japanese Takahashi Hideomi, is certainly not precise. However, in the current situation, compared with 1922, after repeated military disasters and banditry, the national income of the Chinese people has only decreased, and certainly has not increased compared to before. This can be determined by common sense. There are no domestic statistics on the average figure for the tax burden of the Chinese people, but judging from various scattered statistics, there is only a tendency to increase, and no decrease. Taking the burden on farmers alone, according to the statistics of 678 counties in 16 provinces by the Central Agricultural Experimental Institute, the tax rates for paddy fields and dry land in various provinces are as follows:

According to informal surveys, Chen Hansheng estimates that the burden of land tax on Chinese farmers accounts for at least 5% of their total income. According to Feng Jie's "Research on Chinese Land Tax," in the affluent areas of southern Jiangsu, taking Wuxi as an example, land tax accounts for 11% of total income, and in Guangdong and Fujian, land tax accounts for more than 14% of total income. As for the civil war areas of Sichuan and Guizhou, land tax even exceeds total income. In the annual total income of farmers, in addition to the cost of cultivation, plus the burden of land tax, as well as the commodity tax on agricultural products, and the tax shifted to consumer goods, what net income is left? According to Wagner, a German, in 1925 statistics on land tax in various counties of Shandong, and Shen Shanwei's statistics on land tax in various counties of Zhejiang, the burden on farmers is compared with that of farmers in various countries as follows:

The burden on Shandong farmers is:

Four times higher than that of American farmers in 1922

One and a half times higher than that of Indian farmers in 1924

The burden on Zhejiang farmers is:

Sixty times higher than that of Prussian farmers in 1866

Eighteen times higher than that of American farmers in 1920

Eight times higher than that of Japanese farmers in 1931

Since farmers account for the majority of the Chinese population, the high level of burden on farmers fully reflects the extraordinarily heavy tax burden on the Chinese people, and the weakness of their ability to bear burdens in the future. In the tax burden of various countries, industry and commerce also occupy a major position, but in China today, the ability of industry and commerce to bear taxes is also very limited. First, because of the economic bankruptcy of the inland and the reduction of purchasing power, increasing the tax burden on industry and commerce further narrows the market for manufactured goods. Second, China's industry and commerce are currently under heavy pressure from foreign industry and commerce. Increasing the burden on Chinese industry and commerce is tantamount to assisting a tyrant. There is no need to waste words explaining these two points. Just look at the decline of China's new-style industries such as cotton spinning, matches, and cigarettes after the recent increase in consolidated taxes, and it can be seen that industry and commerce have lost their ability to bear taxes.

Let us further observe the income situation of the middle class and salaried class in general Chinese cities and compare it with that of other countries. We can then know that their ability to bear taxes is as weak as that of other classes. The table below is a detailed survey by the International Labor Bureau between 1920 and 1929. The statistics are relatively reliable. The figures for the Chinese part are based on half-year household accounts from 48 families in Beiping, and the survey period was 1926.

Average Number of People in a Family and Monthly Income

(Content of Expenditure, Total Expenditure Equals 100)

According to the first table, it can be seen that the income of the lower middle class and the salaried working class in Chinese cities is very small. According to the second table, the economic situation of the average Chinese family is pathetic. Compared with other countries, income is the lowest, and food expenses account for the largest proportion of expenditure. According to Engel's Law in economics, the poorer the person, the greater the proportion of their food expenses. The life of the average Chinese person is in line with this statement. They have no ability to enjoy the entertainment, education, and life that other civilized people should have. Do they still have the ability to bear a heavier tax burden?

III. Fiscal Expenditure and the People's Ability to Bear Taxes

As mentioned above, although the people bear the same amount of tax, the degree of sacrifice may not be the same. When measuring the people's ability to bear taxes, in addition to considering the country's national wealth and the people's income, it is also necessary to pay attention to the actual situation of finance. The main points are two:

First, it is necessary to pay attention to the situation of national expenditure. If the expenditure is used for production, then the taxes currently collected can still flow into the economic sector, support production undertakings, and cultivate future sources of tax revenue. This can increase national wealth and the people's income. Although the people bear taxes, they will not suffer major sacrifices. This type of expenditure is called the "tax circulation effect" by economists, and the people can afford it. Conversely, if the expenditure is used for wasteful undertakings or undertakings not directly related to production, then the tax circulation effect is completely stopped, and the people only feel the pain of sacrifice. In reality, it destroys the people's ability to bear burdens.

Comparing China with various countries, there is almost a common situation in expenditure, which is the huge amount of military expenditure and debt expenditure. These two types of expenditure are both non-productive. The huge amount of China's military expenditure and debt expenditure is due to the unsettled civil strife. The huge amount of military expenditure and debt expenditure in various countries is partly the result of the European War, and partly the preparation for current national defense. In terms of the meaning of expenditure, it is quite different. The following table lists the percentage of military expenditure and debt expenditure in various countries for comparison.

Percentage of Military Expenditure and Debt Expenditure in Total Expenditure of Various Countries

Note: This table is taken from the "List of National Conditions of Various Countries" compiled by the Japan Cabinet Statistics Bureau. The Chinese figures are calculated from the 1933 budget.

From the above table, it can be seen that although the huge amount of military expenditure and debt expenditure is a common phenomenon in various countries, it is actually the most serious in China. In other words, although China's economy is backward and the people are poor, its non-productive expenditure on finance is the highest among all countries.

Regarding the methods of developing industry and supporting production, in addition to adopting policies on tariffs and exchange rates to protect domestic products, various countries also try to protect them from the aspects of transportation. China is currently completely unable to talk about these things. In the budget items, the national business expenses and construction expenses can barely be called productive expenditures, but the construction is biased towards highways, and the military nature is more important than the economic nature. Although state-owned enterprises belong to productive expenditures, they have little direct benefit to the people's industry today. If we look back at various countries, in addition to the construction of state-owned enterprises being the responsibility of the government, the annual expenditure is not counted, and the subsidy and bonus for private enterprises by the government alone has reached the following figures:

Percentage of Industrial Subsidy Expenditure and Total Expenditure in Various Countries

Statistical Year-book

The current general industry in China is oppressed by the capital goods of the great powers from the outside, and affected by the bankruptcy of the rural areas from the inside, and has entered a period of collapse. If the burden is continuously increased, (please refer to Yin Boduan's short criticism of the 1934 fiscal facilities in the first issue of this newspaper), it will directly make various industries unable to reproduce, which is no different from killing the chicken to get the egg. If this continues, not only will the sacrifice of the people increase day by day, but the government's tax revenue will also run out one day. The simultaneous sharp reduction in the customs, salt, and unified taxes last year in July, August, and September proves that the people's tax burden has reached its limit, and even if the tax rate is increased, it may not be able to collect enough taxes in proportion to the increase in the rate.

(IV) Fiscal Expenditure and People's Income

There is a kind of fiscal expenditure that can be regarded as the people's quasi-income, and it is also very related to the people's ability to bear taxes. This kind of expenditure in various countries is the three kinds of expenses for culture, education, health, and social facilities, and in China, there is only culture and education expenses. The greater the expenditure of these kinds of expenses, the greater the profit enjoyed by the people, which can reduce the people's own consumption burden on this kind of emotion, which is equivalent to the people's income in invisible form. The less the expenditure of this kind of expenses, the greater the education, health, and social undertaking expenses borne by the people themselves, which is equivalent to the people's expenditure in invisible form. Therefore, although the people's tax burden is heavy, if the government can increase the expenditure on this kind of expenses, the degree of sacrifice of the people can also be reduced, and it will not hinder the people's ability to bear taxes.

In addition, the government's pension for the people is also a kind of income for the people. If this kind of expenditure is more, it can certainly increase the welfare of the people. Due to this kind of expenditure, increasing tax revenue will not only fail to increase the degree of sacrifice of the general people, but also stabilize social order and equalize the distribution of the people's wealth. The following table compares this kind of expenditure between China and various countries.

Percentage of Social Expenses and Fiscal Expenditure in Various Countries

Percentage of Pension Expenditure and Fiscal Expenditure in Various Countries

From the comparison in the above table, it can be seen that the ratio of the current financial expenditure in our country that is truly used for the people is very low. As a result, the wealth of society enters the national treasury, and there is no hope of return. The people's sacrifice of paying taxes does not get corresponding compensation. They also have no ability to enjoy the life of cultural people, and have to fall into the stage of poverty, illness, ignorance, and weakness.

Otherwise, the expenditure of national expenses, although there is a difference between productive and non-productive, there is actually no absolute boundary. Non-productive expenditure can sometimes indirectly support production and increase the people's income. For example, the expenditure of expenses in various countries is mostly still in the country, that is, the increase in military expenditure is actually a wasteful nature, and it is also enough to stimulate the prosperity of the domestic heavy industry, thus solving the unemployment problem of some. After our country's industry, heavy industry has not yet reached the point of self-sufficiency. Among the military expenditure, the expenses for the replenishment of new-style machinery and military supplies, aviation construction, etc., are all spent abroad, and there is little benefit to the domestic economy. The construction of public roads belongs to productive expenditure, but the development of roads today is only enough to promote the consumption of Far East kerosene, and this kind of expenditure is actually spent abroad. Since our country's exports are not enough to offset imports, this part of the expenditure is equivalent to the loss of national wealth, which is also a major reason for weakening the economic tax power of the people.

V. Tax System and the People's Ability to Bear Taxes

The tax system is also sufficient to affect the people's tax power. The national tax principle should take the people's tax bearing ability as the standard. If the burden of Wu's tax falls on the heads of the hard-working people, the result is to increase the degree of sacrifice of the people. For the wealthy class, more tax amount, its degree of sacrifice can be reported. Therefore, the same amount of tax also has different effects depending on the source of the tax. In theory, direct taxes are better than indirect taxes, and income taxes are better than consumption taxes. Because the burden of direct taxes is fixed and cannot be shifted, those who pay indirect taxes can shift their tax amount to the poor people. Income tax takes the people's income as the tax standard, which can be suitable for the people's tax bearing ability. Consumption tax. Tax on the property consumed by the people. The burden of tax on the poor should not be consistent with their tax bearing ability. The tax is the income tax imposed on specified income of individuals or corporation and cannot be transferred that is direct tax. Consumption taxes are imposed on consumer goods before they reach the consumers, and finally shifted to the consumers, so they are indirect taxes. In modern countries, direct taxes are becoming more and more important, while our country's taxes rely solely on indirect taxes. The disadvantages of this have been discussed by all wise men, and there is no need to repeat them here. This article only lists the percentage of direct taxes and indirect taxes in the tax revenue of China and foreign countries for comparison.

Percentage of Direct Taxes and Indirect Taxes in the Annual Income of Various Countries

Note… Copied from Statistical Year-Book League of Nation

It is found that the tax revenue in our country is mainly customs, salt, and three taxes, and these three taxes are all consumption taxes. Consumption taxes are not necessarily bad in themselves, but our country's consumption taxes are completely unreasonable. One of the most important principles of consumption tax is to tax luxury goods and exempt daily necessities. Because the poorer the people, the greater the proportion of daily necessities in their consumption expenditure, and the wealthier the people, the smaller the proportion of daily necessities in their consumption expenditure. In order to adapt to the tax power, daily necessities should be exempt from tax. However, in our country's tax revenue, salt tax accounts for more than 20%, and the burden of salt tax almost all falls on the poor. Other indirect taxes, such as customs and unified taxes, are almost all shifted to the common people, and the bureaucrats, rich, and wealthy who sit on their assets bear very little tax.

VI. Tax Situation of Our Country's People

Based on the above observations, although we have not been able to provide an accurate figure to express the tax situation of our country's people, we can obtain a concept of the tax situation of the Chinese people by observing the national wealth, the people's income, fiscal expenditure, and tax system of our country as follows:

(1) Judging from the national wealth and national income, the tax bearing ability of our country's people is lower than that of any country.

(2) Judging from our country's financial expenditure, the government takes more from the people and uses less for the people. There is more non-productive expenditure and less productive expenditure, and the amount spent abroad is not small. Therefore, the people only have sacrifices and get little compensation. The wealth is gradually lost, the source of tax revenue is not cultivated, and the tax bearing ability is gradually reduced.

(3) Judging from the government's debt expenditure, a country collects taxes from the general people every year, and almost one-third of it is used to repay debts, which is no different from sacrificing the wealth of the whole country to support a small number of financial capitalists. Such expenditure not only cannot equalize the distribution of the people's wealth, but also promotes the phenomenon of unequal distribution, and makes the living standard of the majority of people more and more low.

(4) But judging from the content of the tax revenue, the government imposes limited taxes on the wealthy class who have tax ability, and most of the taxes are consumption taxes that can be shifted to the poor.

Indeed, the tax limit of a country's people is flexible. In addition to the material conditions, there are only mental conditions and the background of the times. The sacrifice that cannot be tolerated in peacetime may be tolerated during the national crisis. But to make the people tolerate this sacrifice, the Kuomintang must be able to recognize the meaning of the country and its own responsibilities: (2) the country's tax system must be fair, so that the people have no complaints, (3) and especially the tax burden must not invade the people's minimum living standard. With the low level of knowledge of our country's people, the unfairness of the tax system, and the hardship of the people's lives, there is still no talk of this kind of mental condition.

VII. Observation Method of Tax Limit

In short, the people's tax power is limited. If it exceeds this limit, the people's sacrifice will be too heavy, and it will induce the general economic decline. And the national tax revenue will also flash the phenomenon of tax regression. However, the measurement of the tax burden power cannot be determined solely by the amount of people's income and tax amount. It is also necessary to consider the direction of fiscal expenditure and the content of tax revenue. Because of this kind of comprehensive relationship, it is almost impossible to judge the exact number of the people's tax power limit in advance. However, after reaching the tax power limit, it can naturally be significantly reflected in the general economic world. Our country's economic status is the opposite proof that the people's tax power has reached the highest limit. We" judge whether the people's tax has reached the highest limit afterwards, we can imitate the "German Prosperity Index" made by Xiaowei, and make a Chinese prosperity index without specific number measurement. The materials on which the Daweisi prosperity index is based are as follows:

(1) The total amount of national elm exports, (the decline in exports indicates a decrease in international income, and the decline in imports indicates a recession in domestic purchasing power.)

(2) The ratio of the amount of tax revenue to the increase or decrease in the tax rate. (The increase in taxes, the increase in tax revenue can increase in the same proportion, the customs indicate that the people's tax power has reached the limit, so the phenomenon of tax revenue regression occurs.)

(3) The transport volume of railways and ships. (The decrease in transportation indicates the stagnation of commodity communication, and the failure of mountain construction.) (4) The content of expenditure. (The increase in sleeve subsidies, pension money, and relief expenses indicates that the people are exhausted and the income is reduced.)

(4) The consumption of cigarettes, alcohol, sugar, and coal, and the total amount paid by consumers. (Due to the increase or decrease in the consumption of daily necessities and hobbies, and the prices of these goods, it is possible to observe the prosperity or yin of the people's lives.)

(6) National current statistics, birth statistics, death statistics, and people's mobile statistics, (Due to the changes in the population, it can be indirectly proved by the general economic situation, for example, the increase in the number of farmers leaving the village is the result of the heavy burden of the rural areas.)

(7) The average amount of salt per person. The increase or decrease in the ratio of school-age children to out-of-school children. (These are all side materials for inferring the people's living conditions).

In short, if the collection of tax exceeds a certain limit, the finance and economy will begin to decline at the same time. The decline in finance is the cumulative reduction in tax revenue, and the decline in economy is shown in the reduction in domestic industry and foreign trade, which simultaneously affects the people's consumption life. After a certain period of time, it will disturb the natural increase rate and marriage rate of the population. The use of the prosperity index is to reflect this comprehensive phenomenon. However, this method can only be used as a tool for post-event research and cannot be used for pre-event judgment. The tax power limit is silent and odorless. The responsibility of the financial authorities is to be cautious and careful in advance, and to consider good financial policies, so that the tax burden does not exceed the limit. If you do not work hard to prevent it in advance, and wait until a hundred diseases occur before trying to remedy it, it will be laborious. Even if the remedy is good, it will be burned. Our country's current finances cannot issue more public debt, and it is not easy to increase taxes. To find a way out, we must carefully consider it from all aspects. 1935, 5, 19. At Chaobao Hall

Shen Bao Pharmaceutical Weekly

Scientific Research on Chinese Materia Medica (Part 1) 187

— Notes by Nie Zhinong and Wang Mingding

——Lecture by Dr. Zeng Guangfang, Doctor of Pharmacy——

Currently, Mr. Zeng Guangfang, Director of Medicinal Botany at the Shanghai Institute of Natural Sciences, is a well-known chemist and pharmacologist in the country. He has used chemical methods to analyze and verify Chinese medicines for more than ten years. This lecture is based on his scientific methods over the past ten years to research the experience and insights gained from Chinese Materia Medica. There are many original ideas, I hope the Chinese people pay attention to it.

Recorded by the reporter at Southeast Medical College

(1) Preface (2) Origin of Materia Medica (3) Materia Medica during the Tang and Song Dynasties (4) Materia Medica during the Ming and Qing Dynasties (5) Types of Materia Medica medicines (6) Ingredients of Materia Medica medicines (7) Materia Medica medicines that have undergone scientific research (8) Conclusion

Preface

Today, I am very honored that everyone has come to my office to listen to the lecture.

The research on Materia Medica is very broad. I will now do my best to guide the research and use of my country's existing medicinal materials and Chinese medicine Materia Medica onto a scientific path. Therefore, I would like to discuss this matter today.

From a historical perspective: As early as two or three thousand years ago, there was the fact that Materia Medica was used for treatment; and the name Materia Medica means medicine. It includes three types: animals, plants and minerals. However, at that time, most of the things used to treat diseases were grass roots and tree bark. Therefore: at that time, the word Materia Medica was used to represent it. Later, minerals and animals were also used as medicines for treating diseases: but the word Materia Medica is still used along the same lines. Today's lecture on Materia Medica refers to all medicines.

We in China have always used plant-based medicines to treat diseases. In the West, grass and plants were also the main means of treating diseases in the past. In recent years, science has developed day by day, and the use of medicine has also been continuously improved. For example, the invention of X-rays, radium pills, and endocrine hormones all occupy an important position in medical treatment. This is a well-known fact to medical colleagues. However, their discovery of these new drugs is based on scientific theories and experiments. The research and use of Materia Medica in our country in the past was somewhat different from that in Western countries now. It was mostly based on imagination and experience; it seems that this is still the case now, which is naturally a major obstacle to progress.

We know that there are still many diseases now that do not have specific medicines to deal with and eliminate them. From this perspective, China's original Materia Medica with a long history really needs to be researched and has value. Explaining and confirming its usable raw materials with scientific methods can immediately be applied widely in the world without causing fear. Recently, many sharp-eyed doctors and pharmacists in Japan and the West have begun to pay special attention to our country's medicines and have developed an interest in research: but they are using scientific experimental methods to research and explore. This seems to make us medical personnel living in China feel greatly excited. We have many Chinese Materia Medica literature; we have many Materia Medica specimens in front of us: and there are many Materia Medica that are still being continuously used by Chinese medicine practitioners: so from various perspectives - textual aspects and literature specimen practice, etc., our research on Materia Medica has extremely convenient advantages over Westerners, and can achieve twice the result with half the effort. I believe that all Chinese people who are interested in researching Materia Medica should unite and work hard, and will definitely emit a ray of brilliant light in the world of medicine!

What I want to declare here is that the scientific research of Materia Medica that I am talking about today is naturally not perfect: if there are any shortcomings, please give special instructions.

Origin of Materia Medica

When it comes to the origin of Materia Medica, we must first discuss the term Materia Medica. In what era did it originate? This is worth investigating. Looking back at our country's history, we know that the word Materia Medica is not found in the Records of the Grand Historian; the author of the Records of the Grand Historian was Sima Qian of the Han Dynasty; from this we can know that the term Materia Medica did not exist in the early Han Dynasty. During the Warring States period, everyone knew that Bian Que was a famous doctor of that period, but in Bian Que's time, there was no term Materia Medica either. Judging from the facts: before Emperor Wu of the Han Dynasty, the name Materia Medica did not exist. Later, the words Materia Medica were first recorded in the Records of the Suburban Sacrifices in the Book of Han. Now let's look at the origin of the word Materia Medica in the Book of Han and record it below:

Records of Suburban Sacrifices in the Book of Han (Emperor Cheng of Han, the second year of Jianshi, namely 21 BC)

"More than seventy alchemists, envoys, assistant officials, Materia Medica attendants were all hoofed families"

Art and Literature Records in the Book of Han (Liu Xin)

"Those who prescribe prescriptions know the cold and warm of Materia Medica, the depth of diseases, fake medicine tastes, nourishing because of the air, direct debate on the five bitter flavors, leading to the Qi of water and fire, to open and resolve knots, friendship in peace"

Records of Emperor Ping of Han (the fifth year of the Western Era)

"Solicit from all over the world those who understand lost classics, ancient records, celestial phenomena, calendar calculations, musical scales, elementary school history techniques, alchemy Materia Medica, and those who teach the Five Classics, Analects, Classics, Erya. Issue a sealed edict to the capital"

Biography of Lou Hu during the reign of Wang Mang (the tenth year of the Western Era)

"Hu was young. His father was a doctor. He went in and out of noble families in Chang'an. Hu recited medical classics, Materia Medica prescriptions, and defended one hundred thousand words"

Secondly, regarding the origin of Materia Medica, according to research, it can be divided into three types: (1) immortals and magic; (2) alchemy; (3) there are many medicine names in the Classic of Mountains and Seas.

(1) In ancient times, when it was still a theocracy, it seemed that everything in the human world was dominated by the so-called "gods" in the dark, so at that time, when huge numbers of people suffered from diseases, they sought gods and divination, relying on those unscientific prescriptions to treat and hear about diseases; that period can be said to be the most prosperous period of immortals and magic, and it was also the initial period of the history of Materia Medica, because in the confusion, some so-called therapeutic Materia Medica were sought, and from experience, medicines with actual efficacy were slowly understood.

Figures who had close relationships between immortals, magic, and Materia Medica. Such as Qin Shihuang; because he wanted to maintain his world from the first generation to the ten thousandth generation, he heard that there were immortal medicines of longevity on the islands of Fusang, so he wonderfully dispatched Xu Fu to carry three thousand boys and girls to those islands to seek the immortal prescriptions for longevity. As a result, Xu Fu could not obtain the immortal prescriptions, so he stayed on the three islands with those boys and girls. The three islands are now Japan, so some people say that some of the people in Japan today are descendants of the boys and girls brought out by Xu Fu. Another example is during the reign of Emperor Wu of the Han Dynasty: because Emperor Wu believed in magic very much, the magic of immortals was extremely prosperous at that time, but later, the magic did not work as well as the alchemists said, and Emperor Wu gradually realized that there were many untrustworthy aspects; and at about the same time, Prime Minister Kuang Heng submitted a memorial, believing that the heretical theories of the alchemists were all deceiving and confusing the public and should be banned. From then on, the magic of immortals gradually declined!

Epilepsy and Migraine 188

— Yueqi

—Story of Medicine Ten—

Under certain circumstances - we can only describe these circumstances with the word "stimulation" - a strong impulse emanates from the nerve center, showing considerable symptoms. "Epilepsy" and "Migraine" are the two most famous diseases caused by this. Epilepsy is due to the spontaneous impulses of the motor nerve center: migraine is due to the spontaneous impulses of the sensory nerve center. These two diseases are quite similar. We might as well call migraine the sensory form of epilepsy. Both are periodic symptoms, both are hereditary diseases, and both have prodromal symptoms before an attack.

During an epileptic seizure, due to the unrestrained motor nerve impulses, the patient's whole body contracts, and the muscles contract very strongly. Sometimes, injury to the head above the motor area, penetrating the skull and causing the cells on the brain surface to form scars: this is also a cause of epilepsy. Tumors in the motor area can also cause the same result. This is called "Jacksonian epilepsy" - named after the famous brain surgeon Hughlings Jackson - and can be treated with surgery. The treatment method is to remove the tumor. However, most cases of epilepsy are incurable; there are no organizational changes in the motor nerve cells, not even visible under a microscope, and periodic contractions invade most of the patient's life. Before an attack, there is often a prodromal symptom, which informs the patient: the old illness is about to break out again. The form of the prodromal symptom varies from time to time. Sometimes black spots appear in front of the eyes, sometimes a bell-like sound is heard, sometimes the eyelids spasm, and sometimes a strong emotional excitement is felt. Epilepsy is a historically famous disease because it is often accompanied by great genius. It is said that Napoleon and Caesar both suffered from this disease.

Migraine is one of the most interesting diseases. Regardless of men or women, regardless of strength or weakness, anyone can suffer from this disease; many doctors who are good at self-care also suffer from migraines. They don't know which day they will suffer from migraine; they cannot prevent it, and there is no way to prevent it. But there are prodromal symptoms: some feel unusually happy and excited the day before, and they know full well that they will suffer the next day: some sleep more soundly than usual, and when they wake up, they know that their old enemy will arrive at noon: some hear the distant bell sound so beautiful that it is extraordinary, and when the bell sound subsides, their headache will break out. The most common prodromal symptom is the appearance of colored, tortuous light lines in front of the eyes. Strangely enough, these light lines only appear in half of the visual field. It comes suddenly and goes suddenly. Something in the brain clicks, and the pain is completely gone. Sometimes, after a short nap, the old enemy has left without saying goodbye when they wake up. Migraine is also an incurable disease, and patients have to let it stop on its own; probably, the periodic migraine rarely stops after men reach middle age and women reach menopause.

Common Knowledge Q&A About Diseases 189

— Cheng Hanzhang

(69) Jaundice (Part 1)

(Question, what is jaundice?

(Answer) Jaundice is a general term for diseases in which the skin and mucous membranes are dyed yellow by bile pigment: it contains the meaning of bile color. Most of them are symptoms caused by liver and gallbladder diseases.

(Question) Speaking from the cause, how many types of jaundice are there?

(Answer) There are mechanical jaundice, catarrhal jaundice, toxic jaundice, septic jaundice, and hemolytic jaundice.

(Question) What is the cause of mechanical jaundice?

(Answer) The cause of this type of jaundice lies in the narrowing or blockage of the bile duct. Because bile is easily obstructed by the bile duct and stagnates, it is absorbed into the whole body through blood vessels and lymphatic vessels, causing jaundice.

(Question) What are the reasons for obstructing the bile duct?

(Answer) The reasons for obstruction within the bile duct are gallstones, parasites, coagulated blood, or mucus; the obstruction of the bile duct wall is inflammation, swelling, or scar contraction of the bile duct; outside the bile duct are new growths and tumors.

(Question) What are the symptoms of mechanical jaundice?

(Answer) The conjunctiva of the eyeball turns yellow first, followed by the whole body skin turning yellow, and the palatal mucosa in the mouth also

Page 16

shows obvious yellow staining. The skin is itchy, and secretions, such as urine, sweat, amniotic fluid, etc., all contain bile pigment; milk, phlegm, Wu Ye weeping, mucus, etc. sometimes also contain

(Question) What is the difference in the liver of patients with jaundice?

(Answer) The liver of patients with jaundice is enlarged and its hardness also increases; later it shrinks. Often the enlargement of the gallbladder can be felt. Sometimes splenomegaly is seen.

(Question) What changes occur in the stool of patients?

(Answer) The stool turns grayish-white, constipated, and emits a foul odor that is not easily expelled. This is due to the lack of bile pigment and fat absorption disorders.

(Question) What are the abnormal symptoms of the tongue coating, appetite, and body temperature of patients with mechanical jaundice?

(Answer) The tongue is covered with a thick coating, and appetite is poor. Body temperature is often lower than normal; the pulse rate is also reduced.

(Question) What other symptoms are there?

(Answer) Occasionally there are yellow vision, night blindness: painting blindness, etc. In addition, the body loses weight, and there is bleeding from the skin and mucous membranes (like nosebleeds, bloody stools, or vomiting blood).

(Question) What is the prognosis of mechanical jaundice?

(Answer) It depends on the condition of the original disease and is not necessarily good. If jaundice persists for more than three months, it is probably dangerous. Because it can cause the body to develop cholemia, neurological symptoms, delusions, and coma, etc.

(Question) How should mechanical jaundice be treated?

(Answer) First, it is necessary to treat the cause. Second is diet. That is, eat semi-liquid food every day, avoid fats, spices, and alcoholic beverages. Eat more starches and sugars. Protein foods must also be slightly restricted. Third, medicines; use magnesium sulfate, artificial mineral salt, calomel, etc. When the skin is itchy, use calamine lotion and alcohol, salicylic acid alcohol, etc.: or take bromine preparations and atropine, etc. internally.

Common Knowledge of Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Hygiene 190

— Tang Renjin

(65) Chronic Conjunctivitis

There are many and varied causes of chronic conjunctivitis. They can be divided into seven categories. Namely (1) failure to fully treat acute conjunctivitis. (2) Due to living conditions. Such as frequent contact with dust and soot. Or lack of sleep at night. Or frequent exposure to wind and rain. (3) Due to occupational reasons. Such as stokers and blacksmiths who often work near flames. (4) Living in poorly ventilated, crowded places with many people, and lacking fresh air and with a lot of smoke and dust (such as theaters, hotels, barbershops, cafes, dance halls, school dormitories, public buses, trains, streetcars, factories, etc.). (5) When suffering from astigmatism and hyperopia. (6) Generally, the compatriots who have fallen into the underworld. Lying on opium couches all day long. Living in confined rooms. With lots of smoke and lack of fresh air. (7) Caused by local reasons. Such as foreign bodies, chalazion, trichiasis, eyelid eczema, eyelid inflammation, meibomian gland obstruction, ectropion, lacrimal duct stenosis, and dacryocystitis, etc. All seven of these are sufficient to cause chronic conjunctivitis. Speaking of its symptoms, they are much milder than those of acute conjunctivitis. The ordinary eyelid conjunctiva also becomes congested. The conjunctiva is generally cloudy and thickened. The papillae are enlarged. The conjunctiva is not smooth at all. It becomes rough. Although there is little secretion, the edges of the eyelids are often sticky every morning. Sometimes soap-like foam can be observed on the edges of the eyelids. Sometimes it mixes with tears to form an emulsion. The edges of the eyelids are often red. The appearance is as if crying. Near the corner of the eye. Sometimes skin peeling, cracking, chapping, etc. can occur.

Patients with this disease, in mild cases, may not feel any pain. However, most feel that the eyelids are heavy. It is easy to fatigue when opening the eyes. So the eyes of patients often seem tired and sleepy. In addition, burning, itching, photophobia, frequent blinking, dry eyes, and the sensation of the eyelids sticking to the eyeball, etc. are also common symptoms. These symptoms usually gradually increase from morning to night. So patients feel tired soon after working.

The treatment method for this disease. First, pay attention to eye hygiene. Restrict the use of the eyes. Wear colored glasses to avoid light stimulation. Or use protective glasses to prevent the invasion of smoke and dust. At the same time, improve or eliminate the causes mentioned above. Medical treatment such as (1) If there is acute conjunctivitis. Treat it immediately. Avoid it turning into this disease. (2) Living conditions must be improved. (3) This is a matter of career. (4) Improve ventilation equipment. (5) Correct refractive errors of the eyes. (6) Abstain from addictions. This can protect the eyes and increase longevity. (7) Treat the diseases that cause local reasons.

Q&A on Dental Knowledge (3) 191

— Lin Jianxian

(Question 11) Why do most Chinese people not chew slowly when eating, but prefer to eat quickly? Should this habit be corrected?

(Answer) Chinese people do not understand the importance of digestion in the mouth, so they are unwilling to chew more; they leave their readily available teeth unused, burying their natural function. Some people even use soup to rinse their rice, finishing it in two or three mouthfuls, half swallowing and half drinking. Much of the food eaten in this way is excreted before the stomach and intestines have time to digest it. Eating twice as much food only yields half the nourishment, which is not worth it. Many people eat a lot at each meal, but do not gain weight, and this is the reason. Moreover, because digestion in the mouth is insufficient, the stomach and intestines have to increase their burden. Over time, this leads to indigestion and other gastrointestinal diseases, resulting in a sallow complexion and thinness, which is quite harmful. Therefore, to pay attention to hygiene, the bad habit of eating quickly must be reformed. Each meal should be chewed slowly and thoroughly. Some doctors even advocate chewing each mouthful of rice at least sixty times, until there is nothing left to chew. I hope that everyone, even if they cannot do this, will pay attention to developing the good habit of chewing thoroughly. It is definitely beneficial to health.

(Question 12) How should people with weak stomachs and intestines eat?

(Answer) (1) They should chew thoroughly. (2) They should not use soup or tea to rinse their rice, because rinsing with soup reduces the secretion of saliva and the number of times they chew. (3) There is no need to exclusively choose soft foods such as eggs and milk. Even dry, hard, and coarse foods such as peanuts and hard-shelled fruits can be easily digested and very nourishing if they are chewed thoroughly and not eaten in excessive amounts. There are indeed many people who have cured their gastrointestinal diseases or turned their bodies from weak to strong by developing these good habits.

Section 2 Other Functions of Teeth

(Question 12) What is the function of teeth in pronunciation?

(Answer) Teeth can assist the tongue, making speech fluent and pronunciation accurate. If the front teeth are missing, speech will leak air, which is very inconvenient.

(Question 14) What is the relationship between teeth and appearance?

(Answer) There are two kinds of relationships: indirect and direct. The indirect relationship is that teeth support the muscles of the lips and cheeks, making the face upright. If teeth are lost in youth, the muscles of the lips and cheeks will shrink, and the face will look like an old woman's! The direct relationship is that clean teeth can increase beauty. Who doesn't admire "bright eyes and white teeth"! If one's mouth is full of dirty and uneven teeth, people will find it disgusting and will "avoid it by a mile"! Therefore, teeth have a very close relationship with social interaction.

Chapter 2 Growth of Teeth

Section 1 Growth and Replacement of Deciduous Teeth

(Question 15) How many sets of teeth can a person grow in their lifetime?

(Answer) Two sets: the first set is deciduous teeth, and the second set is permanent teeth.

(Question 16) At what age do deciduous teeth grow?

(Answer) Deciduous teeth grow gradually between the ages of six months and three years after a child is born.

(Question 17) How many deciduous teeth are there in total? What is the order in which they grow?

(Answer) There are twenty in total. The first to emerge are the central incisors, which grow around six to seven months of age. The second are the lateral incisors, which grow around eight to ten months of age. The third are the first molars, which grow around ten to sixteen months of age. The fourth are the canines, which grow around sixteen to twenty months of age. The fifth are the second molars, which grow around twenty to thirty months of age. There is one of each of these five types of teeth on each side of the upper and lower jaws, so there are twenty in total.

Medical Treatment for Pain (34) 192

— Li Xing

Anesthetics

The most important anesthetics are morphine, opium, heroin, codeine, etc., among which morphine occupies the most important position and can be used as a representative of anesthetics. A detailed description is given below:

Morphine

The chemical composition of morphine is C17H19NO3, that is, seventeen carbon molecules, nineteen hydrogen molecules, one nitrogen molecule, and two oxygen molecules. Morphine is also an important component of opium. Dry opium contains about nine percent morphine. Morphine is a fine white powder or fine white crystals, easily soluble in water, with a bitter taste and no odor.

The most important function of morphine in the body is to anesthetize the brain. In the laboratory, testing the effect of morphine on frogs, the result is that the actions of a frog poisoned with morphine are the same as those of a frog with its cerebrum removed. Its effect on other animals and the human body is roughly the same. Therefore, the greatest effect of morphine is to anesthetize sensation. The sensation of pain is located entirely in the cerebrum. Once the cerebrum is anesthetized, both the sensation of pain and ordinary sensations are lost. Now, for example, if a finger is cut off, the pain is very severe. The effect is that a stimulus from the injured area is transmitted to the pain sensation center in the cerebrum, and the injured person feels pain. If the cerebrum is deeply anesthetized, not only will one not know the pain of cutting off a finger, but one will not even know the pain of cutting off a hand or a foot. It must be known that whether one feels pain or not when cutting off a hand or foot, the body is injured in the same way. It is not that being numb and not feeling pain means that there is no injury. In addition to anesthetizing pain, morphine also anesthetizes other sensations, and is also a powerful hypnotic. Addicts seem to feel excitement after injecting morphine, but this is actually an anesthetic effect, which is the deceptive effect of morphine. Now, for example, a person is tormented by mental pain all day long, with anxiety and sleeplessness, and is extremely distressed. But once he becomes insane due to excessive anxiety, he changes his normal state, his anxiety disappears completely, and he shouts and laughs as if he is overjoyed, no longer knowing any pain. The excitatory effect of morphine is similar to this.

Morphine has an obstructive effect on the respiratory system. Small amounts of morphine cause weak breathing, while large amounts of morphine cause respiratory arrest and death. Small amounts of morphine have little effect on blood flow, while large amounts of morphine lower blood pressure and endanger life.

Morphine also has a very important effect on the digestive tract. The most important of these is the constipating effect. It can be said that people with morphine or opium addictions are somewhat constipated, and the greater the addiction, the worse the constipation. It is not uncommon for long-time addicts to have a bowel movement only once every one or two weeks. Morphine-like substances cause constipation by: (1) Morphine tightens the pyloric sphincter, causing food to enter the small intestine from the stomach more slowly, so the intestine is less stimulated and less peristalsis occurs. (2) Morphine-like substances numb the sensory function of the anus. The un-numbed anus has a sensory function, that is, when feces accumulate in the large intestine, it triggers a feeling of urgent defecation, and one must go to the toilet. The numbed anus loses this sensation (due to the cerebrum being anesthetized), so defecation can be arbitrarily delayed for many days. (3) Reducing the peristaltic action of the small and large intestines. This is the biggest reason. During digestion, the remaining residue must move downward through the peristalsis of the small and large intestines. Reducing peristalsis slows down the movement of feces downward, resulting in constipation. Long-time addicts have been constipated for a long time, and their bodies are full of toxins (opium toxins and waste toxins). Naturally, their natural intelligence and nature are completely lost. Where do they still talk about propriety, justice, integrity, and a sense of shame! Ask which addict has ever invented anything. Aside from harming their own families and their own compatriots, how would they know how to do things that are beneficial to society and the country. Most of the time, it is not that their nature is bad, but it is the effect of opium toxins.

The proper and improper uses of morphine

The greatest use of morphine is to temporarily relieve severe pain in a short period of time, but it must be used properly. It must be managed and used by a licensed physician. Using it casually is harmful. Examples of proper use are given below. For example, a person has a rotten leg amputated by surgery. He is indeed in great pain for two or three days after the amputation. If he is injected with a small amount of morphine every day during these days to anesthetize his brain, he will feel less pain. After a few days, when the pain is gone, the morphine can be stopped. This is just an anesthetic effect, and the injury to the body is still the same. Using it for short-term severe pain can be considered a savior of mankind. For example, a person suffering from a cancerous tumor in the late stage is in pain all day long, and the doctor has proven that there is no hope of life. Using anesthesia on him to reduce his suffering during his lifetime is also permissible by humanity. For example, there was a patient who had a cancerous tumor under the throat, and in the late stage, it obstructed breathing, and this person suffocated to death after a few days. Anesthetizing his nerves so that he dies naturally without realizing it is much better than suffocating him to death alive without anesthesia. These are all proper uses of anesthetics.

Morphine should not be used for all long-term pains, such as bone pain, stomach pain, and heart pain. Morphine numbs the brain for only a few hours, and after the numbness passes, one will feel pain again. Note that using morphine and opium to treat these diseases is deceiving oneself. Morphine cannot cure a disease other than its anesthetic effect. If it is used whenever there is pain, although one feels no pain for a short period of time, because the disease is still in the body, one will be tightly bound by anesthetics in an unconscious way, and it will be impossible to stop using them. Opium has the same effect as morphine. All kinds of chronic pain have other harmless treatments, and patients must not fall for anesthetics.

A Brief Discussion of Pulmonary Tuberculosis (68) 193

— Hu Jiayan

Chapter 12 Treatment of Pulmonary Tuberculosis

Section 1 Natural Therapy

This is a very important treatment method! Every patient should strictly adhere to it. Among them, the most important and worthy of special mention is "fresh air"! We know that people's need for air is more important than anything else. Food is used to sustain life, but if one does not eat for a day or two, it will not endanger life. Air is very different, and one cannot live without it for a moment. For patients with this disease, it promotes metabolism, regulates body temperature, and increases the body's physiological defense mechanisms. Indirectly, the general symptoms of this disease can also be alleviated or eliminated as a result. Therefore, it is sometimes more important for patients with pulmonary tuberculosis to breathe fresh air than to see a doctor and take medicine. As for symptomatic drug therapy, that goes without saying! In fact, there are many clinical examples of cures achieved solely by this air therapy, and this is the majority. This kind of unpretentious achievement is especially obvious in patients with early-stage disease, and almost all other treatment methods can be completely abandoned. This treatment method, which seems unremarkable, is actually very beneficial. I hope that people suffering from this disease will keep it in mind.

The implementation of air therapy is almost no easier than in large cities with dense populations: patients only need to stay in fresh air, in places with less wind and more sunlight. The ability of cold to worsen symptoms is definitely not as great as most people expect, and patients do not need to worry too much. In addition, air and climate are not unrelated. In the north, the climate is cold, dry, sunny, with little sunlight, and lots of frost and fog: patients cough more severely, easily catch colds, and have increased body temperature. In the south, the climate is hot, the sunlight is too strong, and the regulation of cold and heat is uneven: patients are more likely to develop heart failure, loss of appetite, and other phenomena. Whether the climate is good or not is an important condition for treating patients with this disease. Therefore, changing places for recuperation sometimes has great success for patients with this disease.

Shenbao Local Supplement

Tan Yan

Idle Talk on "Drama Performances for Disaster Relief" 194

— Lügang

In order to provide relief to the general population of affected disaster victims, the people in Shanghai have initiated a charity relief association, urging everyone to search their pockets for this "righteous act" of rescuing our compatriots. Naturally, everyone is happy to assist in this effort, as the saying goes, "People are not plants, how can they be without feelings?" It is just a pity that due to the economic panic of the past few years, many people have gone bankrupt one after another. As for the poor? Their hearts are willing but their strength is insufficient, and they are afraid that their own Western meals will not be full, let alone benefit others? As for those who are well-fed and well-clothed, they seem to be separated by heaven and hell, and there are quite a few who turn a deaf ear. Naturally, there are also those who are willing to generously donate, plucking a hair to help the masses. However, with such a major disaster, it cannot be alleviated by small amounts of money. As the saying goes, "A cup of water for a cartload of burning firewood," what is the use of that?

Therefore, some people, in addition to generously donating, have also advocated things like "flower selections for disaster relief" and "drama performances for disaster relief," which is naturally easier and more widespread than persuading people to donate. Moreover, at the same time, one is "enjoying oneself and also providing disaster relief," so why shouldn't everyone be happy to do so?

However, since we are not "flower-picking bees," "flower selections" are simply irrelevant to us, and that is naturally a game for the tycoons to play. However, drama performances are different. Even if it is not for disaster relief, we always have to watch plays at ordinary times, and watching plays is not necessarily just for enjoyment. We do not deny that drama has the meaning of educating the public, so drama at least has some influence on our lives. Now that we are going to have "drama performances for disaster relief," it is also more "justified" and "grand" than "flower selections" and the like. However, it is only in name that it is "drama performances for disaster relief," but the content of the play has no "disaster" situation at all. That would be putting too much emphasis on "relief" and neglecting "disaster," because: after watching it, the audience still has no feeling, because they are no different from watching ordinary plays.

I believe that if "drama performances for disaster relief" can truly reflect the disaster situation in the play, then everyone will get a little benefit. Otherwise, the disaster victims receiving relief will inevitably be too wronged, because after all, no one can truly know what kind of painful life they are living! In previous years, there was a film "Raging Torrent" about the floods, and there was also a script "Flood" in the theater, but this year there is nothing. Looking around, one cannot help but feel sad!

A Solitary Song 195

— Lion

I loathe people. Or is it that I am loathed by them? For many days, I have enjoyed being close to solitude, like a wild goose, flying and calling at the same time. Below is a stream of cold water, so merciless, unable to bear the sorrowful chirping, the sorrowful song. But occasionally a feather falls from an old wound, and it will be pushed and rolled by the waves into the deep, unfathomable whirlpool. Where is the sandy beach? On which sandy beach is there no great net of the goose-catcher spread? Tired, tired, but where is the place of rest?

Alright, I will rest on this steep cliff for a while. I no longer seek the sandy beach. Every day I have a silver night, millions of floating stars, a few wisps of wandering, tired, pale yellow clouds that have also stopped flowing. The soft dew moistens the mountain fruits that are maturing. Nature's embrace tolerates my solitude. Nature is not lonely. Nature is not empty. Let me be alone, let me be alone. I have abandoned fame and wealth. I have abandoned the partners who float and sink in the world of sound and color. I hold the bright moon and laugh heartily. Even the owl does not cry at night.

Solitude is not bad. Solitude is not bad. This world, these trees, these green grasses, these ripe red fruits... all seem to be mine. No one competes with me. No one looks askance at me with hateful eyes. No one breathes roughly. Feeling so relaxed, I seem to have transcended my usual self and reached another world. Although this world also does not have a flat, wide road, only I walk leisurely. In this lonely night, I can think about anything, I can think about nothing. The hypocritical things that must be done in the crowd, the hypocritical words that must be said, the hypocritical faces that must be worn, I can now ignore them all. No fetters, no dazzling, no temptations, no hidden arrows, no fraud... none of them exist. My whole body is filled with the joyful feeling of freedom. The freedom that is not easily enjoyed in the crowd, I have obtained in solitude. I enjoy it to the fullest, enjoying the boundless natural blessing. Nature is definitely not as stingy and ungrateful as the crowd.

Don't ask me, no one ask me. My mind has long been exhausted. Let me rest for a while. Let me warm a spring-like gentle dream in the purple solitude. Oh, friend, please don't bother me again. Please don't touch me again with your cold face and burning hands. I can't stand this kind of cold and hot stimulation! Let me see a few fewer tragedies in the grindstone of life, see a few fewer trembling figures of orphans and widows, a spasm-stricken person in the mud, a madman whistling in the hospital bed. Let my heartbeat pause for a while. Let the blood circulation in the heart chamber temporarily achieve harmony. Don't laugh at me, no one laugh at me. I am not afraid of reality and trying to escape. No one can escape reality. But I am tired, tired. I need to rest a bit.

This boundless vastness, this boundless night, I hold my breath, and from silence, I comprehend

Page 18

The eternal law of the universe, the long-hidden dream of life. Everything on the cliff is silent. Only the flocks of birds that have not yet fallen asleep on the treetops are absorbing the fresh nourishment of the natural world. How gentle, how good it is. I am willing to be a blade of grass swaying in the cold stream, a cloud drifting in the sky, or grow wings and fly into a flock of little birds. I do not want the greatness and transcendence of the crowd. Every night, every night, I bathe in the cold moonlight and sing...

Autumn Insects Night Talk 196

— Xiusi

Sitting alone late at night, the sounds of autumn fill the building. At first, I find them annoying, but after a while, they bring me joy.

The neighbor's child was careless somehow, and his cricket ran into my room, calling loudly. I put down my work and searched everywhere, and found it by the window. Originally, I wanted to find the cricket, but when I saw it, I didn't want to catch it, nor did I want to drive it away. I listened quietly to it chirping in the wind, as if I was listening to a great musician singing at the top of his lungs. Unexpectedly, it was not the cricket I was looking for. Another chirping sound rang out in the room, as if two great musicians were singing in harmony. Listening to their singing, one sang in a high register, and the other sang in a low-mid register. They were harmonious, and I was completely intoxicated in their singing, forgetting myself completely.

Some people consider frogs to be the poets of spring. I think crickets are the musicians of autumn. I don't like the poets of spring. Isn't that so? They croak so noisily and monotonously in the ponds. Even when reciting poetry, one should pay attention to rhythm and cadence in order to be considered reciting poetry. Always reciting croak, croak, croak, isn't that boring poetry? I am not a poet and I am not happy to listen to it. Do you think that true poets would willingly acknowledge that frogs are poets?

Frogs are not as good as crickets by ten thousand times. Besides croaking and making noise, they have no other skills. As for crickets? They can sing and they can fight. They are quite like the heroes of the Romantic era, like knights. Wasn't Byron a poet who could fight? However, although crickets are famous for fighting throughout ancient and modern times, it has not been recorded in books whether they fight for the country or the people. I think that crickets' ability to fight is the instinct of living beings to survive. In their place of growth, there may also be distinctions between families, nations, and tribes, and therefore there are also occasional group wars to defend themselves against the oppression of the strong, such as wars for the country and the people. Unlike those who are kept in earthen pots and only act as individualistic, inexplicable heroes.

Crickets can sing and fight. I love crickets.

Talking about crickets reminds me of ants. Aren't ants even more lovable than crickets? Although they are not poets and cannot sing, they are able to endure hardship, explore, and fight, and they fight as a group. They are truly a good model for people. Now it is autumn, and the ants are at their busiest time, storing food for the harsh winter. Summer insects, such as cicadas, although they were proud and happy to sing when their time came, cannot withstand the oppression of the cold wind when summer goes and autumn comes, and they have long sealed their mouths. Crickets, which are able to fight in the autumn wind and sing at the top of their lungs, seem to be more worthy of pride than summer cicadas. However, when autumn goes and winter comes, won't crickets also disappear without a trace? Only ants, their time from spring to summer is a time for enjoyment, and their time from autumn to winter is a time for busyness and hibernation. They are happy and healthy all year round. They are not proud, nor are they sad. They enjoy themselves for life, they fight for life, and they live for life. Isn't that their "view of life"? However, I don't know how long the lifespan of ants is. I love them, and when I think of that, I would like to ask an entomologist.

Autumn ants are busy storing food for the winter, so they often go out to explore. Although they are not autumn insects, they often appear in people's eyes in autumn. In the morning, I saw an ant prowling on my bag of white sugar. I thought that if it went back and reported, it would come with the whole country, and a bag of white sugar would be finished. Just like killing an enemy scout on the battlefield, it is better to kill it than to detain it, so I used my finger to bury it alive in the sugar. Now, when I think of its "personality," it is as if I have done something wrong.

Nighttime Musings 197

— Mo Jia

Watching the green leaves outside the window wither faster and faster, every time I go out, they are scattered all over the ground, adding to the chores of the old gatekeeper. I realize that the autumn atmosphere is gradually thickening and cannot be dispelled. The falling of flowers and leaves seems to be arranged by nature, an irreversible fate. I really lack the elegant mood to lament their misfortune, and I certainly won't have any endless sighs or idle sorrows because of it. Because in my own busy days, I simply can't spare any time to sigh over the passing of spring and mourn the coming of autumn. But recently, I don't know why, I seem to have a kind of rootless emptiness haunting me, always close to me. This emptiness is rapidly swelling, and it has become something weighty on my shoulders, slowly making me feel heavy. So, I often have strange dreams, dreaming that I am a piece of duckweed floating in the vast sea; dreaming that I am a kite stuck in mid-air by the wind, with its string broken and helpless; and dreaming that I am lost and wandering in the dark, dark countryside, hearing faint, fearful howls behind me. With a start, I often wake up like this. When there is moonlight, its faint glow shines on the head of my bed, and I touch my forehead, which is still oozing cold sweat. Recalling the experiences in my dream, I can barely count them, but after careful examination, they are already blurred.

For several nights in a row, it has been like this, and after waking up, it is not easy to fall asleep again. Lying down, listening to the sporadic cries of the night food vendors in the street, or the tail sound of a car speeding past like a gust of wind, I suddenly have two completely different feelings: I can review the cries of the vendors every day, and I am very familiar with those sighing voices. But every time I hear them, I always think of a hard-working person carrying the burden of life, accompanying his own lonely shadow, walking through the desolate streets, desolate alleys, and desolate alleys, sending the long night deeper and deeper. He is carrying a heavy burden and heavy sorrows that no one cares about! Perhaps while my meditation is still unfinished, a loud car horn rushes past again. I know that the car rushing past is carrying the lewd pleasures and joys of some night revelers. When the sound fades away, the faint cries of the vendor float up clearly again. In the lonely night heart, the two sounds blend together. Soon they sink down, and soon they spread up again.

After my dream, my heart is already extraordinarily empty, and now I feel even more fragile, as if tears are about to squeeze out of my eyes. I have no idea why, but when I hear a relatively sharp cry, my heart can't help but tighten, and then beat non-stop. Especially in the silent night, when attacked by the distant dream emotions, and hearing the desolate cries outside, tears really stream down in strings.

Balsam 198

— Hua Zhi

Seeing the scarlet nail polish on the fingernails of urban women, I think of the balsam flowers in my hometown. My late father liked to grow bamboo and raise fish. Those goldfish that he searched for everywhere, carefully collecting and breeding, all died within two months after his death. After a heavy snowy winter, because we were in mourning, no one paid attention to his beloved fish. The fish tank was frozen to the bottom, and the goldfish, like frozen glutinous rice cakes, floated belly up, congealed in the crystal ice, dying for him. There were about a hundred goldfish, divided into categories and stored in three large tanks. When my father was alive, he spent most of his time on them every day. One of them was particularly large, with a left eye like a transparent pearl. It was a variation of the Celestial Eye goldfish, and he said that he was the only one in the whole city who had one. He often invited many friends to his home to see his fish species as an honor. But after he passed away, more than a hundred goldfish, including the only one-eyed dragon in the city, all died. This may have been unexpected by my father. However, the fact that the flower garden is now overgrown with weeds, reaching up to one's shins, is even more unexpected. The flower garden was right in front of my father's bedroom, planted with flowers and plants that bloomed in all seasons. He had different views on flowers and plants. He said that raising goldfish should be valued for their rarity, while flowers should be valued for their abundance, even if it was just grass, as long as it could produce beautiful flowers, my father would cultivate it. Therefore, there were many kinds of flowers in the flower garden for which he made up a name and labeled them with bamboo sticks, treating them the same as noble peonies and gladioli. Friends who came to see his goldfish would naturally also walk around in the flower garden. Seeing him planting flowers in such a "anything goes" manner, they objected, but they could not change my father's prejudice. I remember friends joking with my father, saying that his attitude towards raising fish was like a chaste virgin, but in the flower garden, he was acting like a prostitute. This analogy was very accurate. My father's reply was that a prostitute has a charm different from a virgin, which other flower growers cannot appreciate; this was my father's unique point of view.

The area of the flower garden was very small. Except for a stone-paved walkway in the middle, potted flowers were neatly placed on both sides, and the rest was sown as he pleased. Because my father's view on planting flowers was like this, as long as the flower garden didn't have it, he was very grateful for his friends' gifts. So, the small flower garden was like a flower exhibition, with all kinds of flowers available. But at that time, there were no balsam flowers planted. Until a friend jokingly sent a packet of balsam seeds, my father, without asking why, poured them all into the flower garden, and balsam flowers bloomed. What was strange was that the balsam also mutated, and several plants bloomed with flowers like violets, which he treasured, saying that they were a unique famous flower in our flower garden; he beautifully named them "Violet Balsam," meaning a combination of balsam and violet. But this flower's ability to reproduce was particularly great. Each flower could produce countless fruits the size of olives, and each fruit contained countless seeds. Moreover, without human intervention, when the olive

Page 19

Page 20

Page 21

-shaped fruit burst open, the following year there would be countless balsam flowers. By the third year, the balsam was almost about to invade the entire flower garden. My father could not appreciate that kind of unique "charm" anymore. When they just started to bloom, he almost pulled out seven out of ten. My sisters and I all pounded their flower juice to dye our nails. After that, every year we had to be careful to prune them before they fruited, otherwise next year there would be a garden full of balsam flowers.

After my father passed away, there was no one to manage this flower garden, but the balsam suddenly decreased, and in the second year, it disappeared completely. My mother said that the things my father loved during his lifetime were all sacrificed, and she couldn't help but feel emotional.

Now the flower garden is overgrown with weeds, reaching up to one's shins, and no one cares about it. Thinking about the prosperous situation of pounding balsam flower juice to dye fingernails, how can I not shed tears?

Song Introduction 200

Drought Song

The sun hangs high in the sky, the clouds hide without a trace. The farmers are busy scooping water all day long, and the sun burns their shoulders and backs. Sweat drips, breath pants, the waterwheel goes up and down, the feet are swollen, the crops gradually wither, the water is exhausted, stretching their necks and hoping for rainbows. The fields are difficult to cultivate and the rent is heavy, the farmers suffer endlessly. In the year of drought, there is no harvest, and it is difficult to survive the winter without paying the rent.
