Ballad Singing 202

Zhou Jianhong Yu Kuilong

Dongfang (1020) 11:15 AM to 12:00 AM

Opening Piece "Duke Huan of Qi"

Duke Huan of Qi had a superior spirit, and helped the Zhou Dynasty to unite the world. He forgot grievances for the people and the country. Look at how Guan Zhong once shot at his belt hook. At that time, the brothers were serving the country together, fighting each other without restraint, each fighting for their own master and plotting for their own benefit. Zhao Hu died, Guan Zhong was imprisoned, and the caged car was escorted away without stopping. Fortunately, Bao Shu was a true confidant, persuading Duke Huan not to hold grudges, and leading him into the court as prime minister, and the official military administration was immediately repaired. The Jingman people did not submit to the Zhou system, and blamed the state of Chu for being ashamed of tribute grass. He rescued the state of Wei when it was destroyed, and had nine alliances with the princes in his life. He loved talent and wore his clothes and hats hastily at night, and then took in the poor Ning Qi. It is a pity that he did not listen to the advice of loyal ministers, and three treacherous ministers were in the same class. Prince Kaifang forgot his own country, and Yi Ya killed his son for what he sought. Shushao Yue cut his body and was inhumane. Later, they really rebelled together, and Duke Huan's illness did not subside. He lay in his coffin for sixty-seven days, and his throat was cut off from food and drink during his lifetime. It was too late to regret it, and he was worried even in death.

Gan Fangzhou Li Liansun Mao Jiashou

Huamei (1060) 3:00 PM to 3:45 PM

Opening Piece "Lotus Young Master's Self-Lament"

Monthly roses have just met the long summer days, and the lotus young master is wandering on the embankment. A pair of lotus flowers bloom for a good night's banquet, and willow catkins fly everywhere in madness. Evening primroses show deep affection, and the Dark Wave Magpie Bridge leads the Cowherd. The poppy is inherently frivolous, failing to live up to the Lingxiao cloud rain scene. Hibiscus loves the thinness of yellow chrysanthemums, and the Yellow Millet Dream has not yet awakened at noon. The opium is originally more poisonous than poison, and the weak qualities of Xunlan cannot bear it. Twenty crouching under the pomegranate skirt, the red apricots out of the wall are too absurd. In the unlucky leap year, the boxwood is in a hurry, and the dodder is most heartbroken to be unable to entrust itself. Worldly feelings are even thinner than mallows, and people's faces and peach blossoms sigh at Wang Yang. Slowly arrange the cockscomb and sigh for food, the young man's self-lament is full of meaning. Who is working hard for the fruitless Buddha's hand, and the fate of empty glory is not long-lasting. The wooden pen has no flowers to invest in, and the gourd breaks and the wish is difficult to fulfill. The bloody cuckoo bird emptily complains, and the pear blossoms in the wind and rain are jealous of the delicate girl. The plum contains sourness to awaken, and it is regrettable that the evening fragrance has passed. From now on, the sunflowers must be sincere, and they smell the fragrance and dance to welcome the spring light. The crane son and plum wife will always celebrate the occasion.

Movies

"Three Daughters-in-Law" Released 203

The Kuailelin Company's new film "Three Daughters-in-Law" was released yesterday at the Central Grand Theater in this city. The film depicts the experiences and endings of three different types of daughters-in-law. It has a very accurate satire and praise for women who are wandering in the modern new trend. The film is directed by Wang Tian, starring Xu Suzhen, Chen Yan, Bai Ye, He Zhigang, and Qin Tong. All the music, singing, and dubbing are rare in the small company's position.

Silver Jottings 204

— Zhi Er

The rules of the film industry's charity entertainment event: female stars dance for ten yuan a dance, and dancers dance for one yuan a dance.

Where do the ticket prices for the "film and dance exchange" figures such as Qiao Chen Jingfang, the Liang sisters, and Tan Xuerong come from? (I heard that the film industry's charity entertainment event held a discussion with female stars at the Da Hu last night to discuss dance accompaniment methods. For more details, please see tomorrow's newspaper.)

Camera says: "Wang Junda said that he wanted to "add eye consciousness" in the play, while Chen Dabe's "Xi Shi" said in the advertisement that there was "beautiful salt" consciousness. I would like to say to Mr. Wang that if you want "consciousness one," you can purchase it from Mr. Chen, because Mr. Chen has a lot of "beautiful salt consciousness" in stock (?)"

Not for grabbing business, if Mr. Wang needs other "consciousness" besides purchasing "beautiful salt consciousness," then the author dares to "recommend" to Mr. Wang with "one hundred percent" "serious, frank, and objective":

In the art world, there is "serious consciousness" and "great consciousness" for sale. This kind of "consciousness one paired with a tragic star type one of Wang Meiyu is really more suitable.

Soon, a kind of consciousness will be like medicine, "beautiful salt consciousness" six qian, "serious consciousness" three fen, "great consciousness" five li. In this way, Mr. Chen Dabe became a screenwriter."

However, I don't know if the Chinese film industry, which is taking medicine, will hire a doctor until the impermanence at that time?

From the Importance of Sound Effects to the Sound Effects of "The Tempest" 205

— Qing Yun

Sound effects are an essential element in sound films to promote the development of the plot. To achieve perfection in atmosphere and tone in a sound film, attention must be paid to sound effects, which cannot be ignored. On the contrary, when the plot develops to the climax of tension, if this suitable "sound effect for the development of the plot to the climax of tension" is not used, it will not only lose its due effect, but also destroy the original tension of the plot. Similarly, if the original plot lacks tension, adding suitable and perfect sound effects will inevitably easily capture the emotions of the audience.

Sound films produced in Europe and the United States understand the importance of the connection between sound effects and sound films, so they pay very attention to the sound effects of other sound films. But looking back at our Chinese sound films? Most of them only pay attention to the songs in the sound film, and many of the songs in the sound film have nothing to do with the plot at all, and are forcibly inserted into it. The so-called "attention" is only to cater to the trend of every film having a song. As for sound effects, they are ignored.

It is very gratifying that in today's sound film industry where every film must have a song and ignores sound effects, the Huayi-produced sound film "The Tempest" directed by Yuan Congmei, which is about to be released, is a unique exception that pays attention to the effect of sound effects. It does not focus on songs, but uses perfect sound effects to supplement the progress of the plot. The result of the trial performance, although it has not reached the point of perfection, is still worth exaggerating to say that the sound effect processing of "The Tempest" is quite successful; as for "The Tempest" having no song, it is not because of paying attention to sound effects and ignoring the song, but entirely because the plot does not need it.

Start of the Huai River Project 206

"Water Kingdom Spring and Autumn" Sets Off

The millions of workers in this Huai River project are farmers from nearby counties. Therefore, during the two periods of spring planting and autumn harvesting, they have to temporarily put down their work to busy themselves with their farm work. But once the farm work is completed, everyone will enthusiastically come out and work as usual. Now that the autumn harvest is over, the project office has scheduled the start of construction on the 10th of next month (October). The China Film Company's "Water Kingdom Spring and Autumn" location shooting team will also be led by the film's director, Mr. Wan Wancang, at that time, with a large number of personnel going there. It is expected that the harvest will definitely return with a triumphant song.

Microphone Broadcasting 207

Zhang Shichuan and Zhang Jinde have returned to Shanghai yesterday. According to Dong Keyi, in addition to the dozens of beautiful shots in "Peach Blossoms After the Robbery" in Qingdao this time, there are also several hundred feet of scenery films that have been shot.

On Qiqi Road in the French Concession, there is a Qiqi Tennis Club, organized by several actors, directors, sound engineers, and photographers in the film industry, such as Tang Jie, the "Mr. Wang" of the New Era, Zuo Ming, and Liu Jiqun of Lianhua, all of whom are members. Every morning, they always practice. The day before yesterday, they actually went out to fight the Rong team, and as a result, they returned to the dynasty.

A play directed by Yu Zhongying, director of the Nanjing Central Photography Studio, is named "Rebirth." Most of the actors are actors from various companies in Shanghai. It is said that Jia Nong, Wang Guilin, and Li Junpan are all in it.

In Hu Die's starring "Night Fragrance," Shu Xiuwen, Sun Min, and Zhao Dan all have important positions. According to reliable news, "Night Fragrance" is scheduled to be released at the New Light Grand Theater within three days.

The Wan brothers, Lai Ming, Gu Chan, and Chao Chen, who are the only cartoon book writers in China with a long-standing reputation, have recently, in addition to the cartoon drawings in various Mingxing films, also had a sound cartoon in Diantong's "Urban Scenery." They are now also making a comical cartoon for Xinshengdai's "Mr. Wang Goes to the Countryside," the content of which is Mr. Wang fighting the mosquito soldiers, which is extremely comical.
